===== VIEW dbo._TrafficForDay =====
CREATE   view dbo._TrafficForDay as
Select P.Cod_User,
dbo.GetRightDate(P.Data, O.Inizio,0) Data, -1 Ora,
sum( Dbo.MyMin(O.Fine, (P.Ora + P.Duration)) -
Dbo.MyMax(O.Inizio, P.Ora) ) Totale, P.Split
from TPalinse P with (nolock)
join Traffic_Hour O with(nolock) on (O.Cod_User = P.Cod_User and(
(P.Ora >= O.Inizio and P.Ora <= O.Fine) or
((P.Ora + P.Duration) >= O.Inizio and (P.Ora + P.Duration) <= O.Fine)))
join Tipologie T with (nolock)  on T.Cod_Type = P.NewType
left join TrafficTPalinse TP on TP.ID_TPalinse = P.ID_TPalinse
where (T.Affollamento = 'S' or T.Affollamento = 'G')
and (P.Livello = 0 or (TP.Livello <> 0 and DateDiff(d, GetDate(), TP.Scadenza) >= 0))
and O.Ora >= 100
group by P.Data, P.Cod_User, O.Inizio, O.Ora, P.Split

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.Anagraf_DelVirtualDocument =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[Anagraf_DelVirtualDocument] ON [dbo].[ANAGRAF]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  begin tran
    declare @id int
    declare documents cursor for select ID_VIRTUALDOCUMENT from deleted
    open documents
    fetch next from documents into @id
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@id > 0) exec dbo.Delete_Documento_Virtuale  @id
      fetch next from documents into @id
    end
    close documents
    deallocate documents
  commit tran

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.anagraf_lastupdate =====
CREATE   TRIGGER anagraf_lastupdate
on anagraf
for update
--not for replication
as
	set nocount on
	if (not update(lastupdate)) and
	   (not update(lastuserID))
	begin
		update A set A.lastupdate = getdate(), A.lastuserID = dbo.EtereUserID() 
		from anagraf A 
		join inserted on inserted.id_anagraf = A.id_anagraf
	end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.anagraf_owner =====
CREATE   TRIGGER anagraf_owner
on anagraf
for insert
--not for replication
as
	set nocount on
	update A set A.[ownerID] = dbo.EtereUserID()
	from anagraf A 
	join inserted on inserted.id_anagraf = A.id_anagraf

===== VIEW dbo.arc_wf_log =====
create view arc_wf_log as 
            select
                [id_log],
                [action_ucode] collate database_default as [action_ucode],
                [instance_ucode] collate database_default as [instance_ucode],
                [state_ucode] collate database_default as [state_ucode],
                [foreign_ucode] collate database_default as [foreign_ucode],
                [foreign_key],
                [id_job],
                [id_action],
                [id_instance],
                [id_state],
                [operation] collate database_default as [operation],
                [runtime_data] collate database_default as [runtime_data],
                [timestamp],
                [result],
                [message] collate database_default as [message],
                [worker_info] collate database_default as [worker_info],
                [worker_loginname] collate database_default as [worker_loginname],
                [worker_cod_user],
                [runtime_status],
                [os_login] collate database_default as [os_login],
                [hostname] collate database_default as [hostname],
                [program_name] collate database_default as [program_name],
                [hostprocess] collate database_default as [hostprocess]
            from wf_log

===== VIEW dbo.arc_wf_logInfo =====
CREATE view arc_wf_logInfo as select  WI.id_instance as ID_INSTANCE, WL.id_log as ID_LOG, WA.id_action as ID_ACTION, WAC.id_actionclass as ID_ACTIONCLASS, WAC.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME, WAC.category1 as ACTIONCLASS_CATEGORY, WI.foreign_key AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_KEY, WL.worker_loginname AS WORKER_LOGINNAME,  WS.friendly_name as StateName, WL.id_state, WL.timestamp, WL.result, WL.message, WL.os_login, WL.hostname, WL.program_name, WL.hostprocess, WL.worker_cod_user, WI.id_instanceclass as ID_INSTANCECLASS, WFO.Ucode AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_CODE from wf_instance	WI with (nolock) join arc_wf_log	WL with (nolock) on WL.id_instance = WI.id_instance join wf_action	WA with (nolock) on WL.id_action = WA.id_action join wf_actionclass 	WAC with (nolock) on WAC.id_actionclass = WA.id_actionclass join wf_state		WS with (nolock) on WL.id_state = WS.id_state  join wf_foreignobject 	WFO with (nolock) on WI.id_foreignobject = WFO.id_foreignobject

===== VIEW dbo.ClusterTPalinse =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[ClusterTPalinse]
AS
SELECT     MIN(a.ID_TPALINSE) id_tpalinse, a.COD_USER, a.LIVELLO, a.DATA, a.DATA_P, a.ORA_P, MIN(a.ORA) AS ORA, 
           SUM(a.DURATION) AS DURATION, dbo.fn_codBreak(min(newtype)) cod_progra, 0 timecode_i, 
           sum(duration) timecode_o, '' title
FROM         dbo.tpalinse a LEFT OUTER JOIN
--dbo.tipologie t ON t.COD_TYPE = a.NEWTYPE LEFT OUTER JOIN
dbo.tipologieprop P ON P.COD_TYPE = a.NEWTYPE
WHERE     (P.PROP = 'oiRaggruppaInCluster')
GROUP BY a.DATA, a.COD_USER, a.LIVELLO, a.DATA_P, a.ORA_P

===== VIEW dbo.DataContract =====
CREATE   View dbo.DataContract as
Select CT.ID_ContrattiTestata,
	CT.Cod_Contratto ContractCode, CT.Descrizione ContractDescription, 
	Comm.Cod_Conto CostumerCode, Comm.Rag_Social CostumerDescription,
	Ag.Cod_Conto AgencyCode, Ag.Rag_Social AgencyDescription,
	UF.Cod_Conto FinalUserCode, Uf.Rag_Social FinalUserDescription,
	CM.Cod_Conto MediaCenterCode, CM.Rag_Social MediaCenterDescription,
	CT.Data_Acquisizione ContractDate,   Month(CT.Data_Acquisizione) ContractMonth, Year(CT.Data_Acquisizione) ContractYear,
	CT.Data_Inizio ContractStartingDate, CT.Data_Termine ContractEndingDate,
	Ag1.Cod_Conto Ag1Code, Ag1.Rag_Social Ag1Description,Ag2.Cod_Conto Ag2Code, Ag2.Rag_Social Ag2Description,
	Ag3.Cod_Conto Ag3Code, Ag3.Rag_Social Ag3Description,Ag4.Cod_Conto Ag4Code, Ag4.Rag_Social Ag4Description,
	Ag5.Cod_Conto Ag5Code, Ag5.Rag_Social Ag5Description,
	CR.ID_ContrattiRighe, CR.Descrizione RowDescription,
	N.Nielsen CategoryCode, N.Descrizione CategoryDescription,
	CR.Prenotazione SchedulingType, CR.Cod_User UserCode, CR.N_Passaggi SchedulingCount, 
	CR.Importo SchedulingPrice, (CR.Importo * CR.N_Passaggi) SchedulingTotalPrice, CR.Omaggio FreePriceScheduling,
	dbo.NullToZero(Sch.Scheduled) Scheduled, dbo.NullToZero(Res.Reserved) Reserved,
	(CR.N_Passaggi - dbo.NullToZero(Sch.Scheduled) - dbo.NullToZero(Res.Reserved)) SchedulingRemain ,
	CT.Rate DeferredPayment, dbo.GetTotaleSpese(CR.ID_ContrattiRighe) TotalCharges
	from ContrattiTestata CT with (nolock)
	left join Anagraf Comm with (nolock) on Comm.ID_Anagraf = CT.Committente
	left join Anagraf Ag   with (nolock) on Ag.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agenzia
	left join Anagraf Uf   with (nolock) on Uf.ID_Anagraf = CT.Ut_Finale
	left join Anagraf Cm   with (nolock) on Cm.ID_Anagraf = CT.CentroMedia
	left join Anagraf Ag1  with (nolock) on Ag1.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agente1
	left join Anagraf Ag2  with (nolock) on Ag2.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agente2
	left join Anagraf Ag3  with (nolock) on Ag3.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agente3
	left join Anagraf Ag4  with (nolock) on Ag4.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agente4
	left join Anagraf Ag5  with (nolock) on Ag5.ID_Anagraf = CT.Agente5
	left join ContrattiRighe CR with (nolock) on CT.ID_ContrattiTestata = CR.ID_ContrattiTestata
	left join Nielsen N    with (nolock) on N.Nielsen = CR.Nielsen
	left join (Select ID_ContrattiRighe, Count(ID_ContrattiRighe) Scheduled from TrafficTPalinse where Livello = 0
		   group by ID_ContrattiRighe) Sch on Sch.ID_ContrattiRighe = CR.ID_ContrattiRighe
	left join (Select ID_ContrattiRighe, Count(ID_ContrattiRighe) Reserved from TrafficTPalinse where Livello = 10000
		   group by ID_ContrattiRighe) Res on Res.ID_ContrattiRighe = CR.ID_ContrattiRighe

===== SQL_STORED_PROCEDURE dbo.DeleteTpalinse =====
CREATE procedure dbo.DeleteTpalinse @id_filmati int as delete from tpalinse where id_filmati = @id_filmati

===== VIEW dbo.ENVOICELIST =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[ENVOICELIST] AS
	SELECT F.ID_FatturaTestata , F.Numero, F.Data, A.Rag_Social Cliente_Fattura, A.Cod_Conto Cod_Cliente_Fattura, 
	       F.Proforma, F.Cod_User, F.NotaCredito, F.ID_cliente, F.Anno_Rif, F.Acconto,
	       C.Agenzia,C.P_Agenzia,C.Agente1,C.P_Agente1,C.Agente2,C.P_Agente2,C.Agente3,C.P_Agente3,
	       C.Agente4,C.P_Agente4,C.Agente5,C.P_Agente5,dbo.trf_calcTotSpeseContra(C.id_contrattitestata) SpeseContratto,c.invoicemode,
	       dbo.trf_getTotImponibileFattura(F.Id_fatturatestata) totaleImpoFattura,F.MODULE,F.NOTE,F.id_contrattitestata,F.ID_DOCTYPE
	FROM FATTURATESTATA F
	LEFT JOIN ANAGRAF A ON F.ID_Cliente = A.ID_Anagraf
	LEFT JOIN CONTRATTITESTATA C ON C.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA=F.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.fedldescription_schedule_checksum =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[fedldescription_schedule_checksum] ON [dbo].[fedldescription]
for INSERT, UPDATE 
as
begin
	declare @id_filmati int
	declare @version int
	declare @chks1 int
	declare @chks2 int
	declare checksum_changed_edl cursor for 
		select id_filmati,version from inserted 
		group by id_filmati, version
	open checksum_changed_edl
	fetch next from checksum_changed_edl into @id_filmati, @version
	while @@fetch_status=0
	begin
		select @chks1=schedule_checksum from fedldescription with (nolock) where id_filmati=@id_filmati and version=@version
		exec dbo.UpdateScheduleCheckSum_FEdlDescription @id_filmati, @version
		select @chks2=schedule_checksum from fedldescription with (nolock) where id_filmati=@id_filmati and version=@version
		if (@chks1<>@chks2)
		begin
			exec dbo.wf_runtime_afterAssetUpdate @id_filmati
		end
		fetch next from checksum_changed_edl into @id_filmati, @version
	end
	close checksum_changed_edl
	deallocate checksum_changed_edl
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.Filmati_DelSecEvents =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[Filmati_DelSecEvents] ON [dbo].[FILMATI]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  begin tran
    declare @id int
    declare SecEvents cursor for select id_filmati from deleted 
    open SecEvents
    fetch next from SecEvents into @id
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      delete from fsec where id_event=@id
      fetch next from SecEvents into @id   
    end 
    close SecEvents
    deallocate SecEvents
  commit tran

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.Filmati_DelVirtualDocument =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[Filmati_DelVirtualDocument] ON [dbo].[FILMATI]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  begin tran
    declare @id int
    declare documents cursor for select ID_VIRTUALDOCUMENT from deleted
    open documents
    fetch next from documents into @id
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@id > 0) exec dbo.Delete_Documento_Virtuale  @id
      fetch next from documents into @id
    end
    close documents
    deallocate documents
  commit tran

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.filmati_lastupdate =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[filmati_lastupdate] ON [dbo].[filmati]
FOR INSERT, UPDATE /*, DELETE */
AS
begin
	if not update(lastupdate) 
	begin
		declare @count int
		select @count = count(*) from inserted
		if @count>0
		begin
			declare @id_filmati int
			declare id_filmati_changed cursor for select id_filmati from inserted
			open id_filmati_changed
			fetch next from id_filmati_changed into @id_filmati
			while @@fetch_status=0
			begin
				update filmati set lastupdate=getdate() where id_filmati=@id_filmati
				exec dbo.UpdateScheduleCheckSum_Filmati @id_filmati
	
				exec dbo.wf_runtime_afterAssetUpdate @id_filmati
				fetch next from id_filmati_changed into @id_filmati
			end
			close id_filmati_changed
			deallocate id_filmati_changed
		end
	end
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.Filmati_Update_Marks =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[Filmati_Update_Marks] ON [dbo].[filmati]
FOR UPDATE
AS
begin
-- Changing pos_ini or pos_fin or durata, the trigger updates som, eom, duration in FEdlDescription
set nocount on
if (update (pos_ini) or update (pos_fin) or update (durata))
begin
	if Exists(select * from FEdlDescription F with (nolock) 
					join Inserted I on I.ID_Filmati = F.ID_Filmati
					where F.version=0)
	begin
		update F with (rowlock) set
		som = pos_ini,
		eom = pos_fin,
		duration = durata
		from FEdlDescription F
		join Inserted I on I.ID_Filmati = F.ID_Filmati and F.version=0
		where (pos_ini<>som or pos_fin<>eom or durata<>duration)		
	end 
end
set nocount off
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.finterruzioni_schedule_checksum =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[finterruzioni_schedule_checksum] ON [dbo].[finterruzioni]
for INSERT, UPDATE , DELETE 
as
begin
	update fe set schedule_checksum=-1
	from fedldescription fe
	join 
		(
		select id_filmati, version from (
			select id_filmati, version from inserted 
				union 
			select id_filmati, version from deleted
			) t
		group by id_filmati, version
		) fi on fe.id_filmati=fi.id_filmati and fe.version=fi.version
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.flink_lastupdate =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[flink_lastupdate] ON [dbo].[flink]
FOR INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
begin
	begin try
		update f set
			lastupdate=GETDATE()
		from filmati f with (rowlock)
		join inserted i on f.id_filmati=i.Id_Filmati1
		update f set
			lastupdate=GETDATE()
		from filmati f with (rowlock)
		join inserted i on f.id_filmati=i.Id_Filmati2
		update f set
			lastupdate=GETDATE()
		from filmati f with (rowlock)
		join deleted i on f.id_filmati=i.Id_Filmati1
		update f set
			lastupdate=GETDATE()
		from filmati f with (rowlock)
		join deleted i on f.id_filmati=i.Id_Filmati2
	end try
	begin catch
	end catch
end

===== VIEW dbo.foreign_keys =====
CREATE   view dbo.foreign_keys as
   select cast(f.name  as varchar(255)) as fk_name
    , r.keycnt
    , cast(ft.name as  varchar(255)) as foreign_table
    , cast(f1.name as varchar(255))  as foreign_col1
    , cast(f2.name as varchar(255))  as foreign_col2
    , cast(pt.name as varchar(255))  as primary_table
    , cast(p1.name as varchar(255))  as primary_col1
    , cast(p2.name as varchar(255))  as primary_col2
    from sysobjects f
    inner join sysobjects ft on  f.parent_obj = ft.id
    inner join sysreferences r on f.id =  r.constid
    inner join sysobjects pt on r.rkeyid = pt.id
    inner  join syscolumns p1 on r.rkeyid = p1.id and r.rkey1 = p1.colid
    inner  join syscolumns f1 on r.fkeyid = f1.id and r.fkey1 = f1.colid
    left join  syscolumns p2 on r.rkeyid = p2.id and r.rkey2 = p1.colid
    left join  syscolumns f2 on r.fkeyid = f2.id and r.fkey2 = f1.colid
    where f.type =  'F'
/* babelfish version also valid for MS SQL **
SELECT
    fk.name AS fk_name,
    COALESCE(1 + CASE WHEN fkc2.parent_column_id IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 1) AS keycnt,
    ft.name AS foreign_table,
    fc1.name AS foreign_col1,
    fc2.name AS foreign_col2,
    pt.name AS primary_table,
    pc1.name AS primary_col1,
    pc2.name AS primary_col2
FROM sys.foreign_keys fk
JOIN sys.tables ft ON fk.parent_object_id = ft.object_id
JOIN sys.tables pt ON fk.referenced_object_id = pt.object_id
JOIN sys.foreign_key_columns fkc1 ON fk.object_id = fkc1.constraint_object_id
JOIN sys.columns fc1 ON fkc1.parent_column_id = fc1.column_id AND fkc1.parent_object_id = fc1.object_id
JOIN sys.columns pc1 ON fkc1.referenced_column_id = pc1.column_id AND fkc1.referenced_object_id = pc1.object_id
LEFT JOIN sys.foreign_key_columns fkc2 ON fk.object_id = fkc2.constraint_object_id AND fkc2.parent_column_id != fkc1.parent_column_id
LEFT JOIN sys.columns fc2 ON fkc2.parent_column_id = fc2.column_id AND fkc2.parent_object_id = fc2.object_id
LEFT JOIN sys.columns pc2 ON fkc2.referenced_column_id = pc2.column_id AND fkc2.referenced_object_id = pc2.object_id
** */

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.FS_BASEPATH#AF_IU#SYNC_FULL_PATHNAME =====
CREATE TRIGGER [FS_BASEPATH#AF_IU#SYNC_FULL_PATHNAME] ON [FS_BASEPATH] 
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE 
NOT FOR REPLICATION
AS 
  IF UPDATE([BASEPATH]) BEGIN
    UPDATE P WITH (ROWLOCK)
      SET P.[FULL_PATHNAME] = [dbo].[fs_getFullPathname](P.ID_PATH)
      FROM [FS_PATH] P 
         JOIN INSERTED I ON P.ID_BASEPATH = I.ID_BASEPATH
  END

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.FS_BASEPATH#FO_IU#CHECK_UNIQUE =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [FS_BASEPATH#FO_IU#CHECK_UNIQUE] ON [FS_BASEPATH]
FOR INSERT, UPDATE
--NOT FOR REPLICATION
AS 
  IF UPDATE([BASEPATH]) BEGIN
    DECLARE @CNT INT
    DECLARE @S NVARCHAR(MAX)
    SELECT @CNT = COUNT(*), @S = MAX(BASEPATH) FROM FS_BASEPATH BP
    WHERE BP.BASEPATH IN (SELECT BASEPATH FROM INSERTED) AND 
          LEN(ISNULL(BP.BASEPATH , '')) > 0 AND
          BP.ID_BASEPATH NOT IN (SELECT ID_BASEPATH FROM INSERTED)
    IF (@CNT > 0) BEGIN
        RAISERROR ('Cannot insert duplicate [BASEPATH]', 16, 1)
        IF @@TRANCOUNT > 0 ROLLBACK TRAN
    END
  END

===== VIEW dbo.FS_DIRECTORY =====
CREATE   VIEW FS_DIRECTORY
AS
  SELECT 
    MF.ID_METAFILE, 
    MD.ID_METADEVICE, 
    FL.ID_FILE, 
    FF.ID_FILMATI,
    FP.ID_PATH,
    FP.ID_BASEPATH,
    MF.[FILE_ID],
    MF.SOM, 
    MF.DUR,
    MF.FLAG_OFFLINE, 
    MF.ID_CODEC,
    FL.[FILE_NAME] AS PHYSICAL_FILENAME, 
    FL.[SIZE] AS PHYSICAL_SIZE, 
    FP.FULL_PATHNAME AS PHYSICAL_PATHNAME 
  FROM FS_METAFILE MF WITH (NOLOCK)
        JOIN FS_METADEVICE MD WITH (NOLOCK) ON MF.ID_METADEVICE = MD.ID_METADEVICE
        LEFT JOIN FS_XFILEFILM FF WITH (NOLOCK) ON FF.ID_METAFILE = MF.ID_METAFILE
        LEFT JOIN FS_FILE FL WITH (NOLOCK) ON MF.ID_METAFILE = FL.ID_METAFILE
        LEFT JOIN FS_PATH FP WITH (NOLOCK) ON FL.ID_PATH = FP.ID_PATH

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.fs_file#iu#check_offline =====
create trigger [fs_file#iu#check_offline] on [fs_file] 
for insert, update 
not for replication
as 
  if update([id_path]) begin
    if exists(  select flag_offline 
                from fs_basepath bp
                    join fs_path fp on fp.id_basepath = bp.id_basepath
                    join inserted i on i.id_path = fp.id_path
                where bp.flag_offline = 1
              ) begin  
      raiserror ('cannot link a file to an offline path', 16, 1)
      rollback tran
    end
  end

===== VIEW dbo.FS_FILMATI =====
CREATE   VIEW FS_FILMATI
AS
  SELECT 
    MF.ID_METAFILE, 
    MD.ID_METADEVICE, 
    FI.ID_FILMATI,
    FI.ID_SERIE,
    MF.ID_CODEC,
    CO.TYPE AS CODEC_TYPE,
    isnull(copv1.value,cop1.defaultvalue) as CODEC_PROXY,
    isnull(copv2.value,cop2.defaultvalue) as PROXY_DEFAULT,
    isnull(copv3.value,cop3.defaultvalue) as PLAYER,
    CO.VIDEOSTD AS VIDEOSTANDARD,   
    MD.[LEGACY_BASESUPP] AS LEGACY_BASESUPP,
    MD.rs_cd_media,
    MF.[FILE_ID],
    MF.SOM, 
    MF.DUR,
    MF.FLAG_OFFLINE, 
    FI.COD_PROGRA,
    FI.DESCRIZIO,
    FI.POS_INI,
    FI.POS_FIN,
    FI.NEWTYPE,
    FI.LASTUPDATE,
    FL.[FILE_NAME] AS PHYSICAL_FILENAME, 
    FL.[SIZE] AS PHYSICAL_SIZE, 
    FL.[ID_FILE] AS ID_FILE, 
    FP.ID_PATH, 
    FP.FULL_PATHNAME AS PHYSICAL_PATHNAME ,
    FL.EXT_SUBPATH , 
    FL.EXT_FILE_NAME ,
    MF.EXPIRY_DATE
  FROM FS_METAFILE MF WITH (NOLOCK)
        JOIN FS_METADEVICE MD WITH (NOLOCK) ON MF.ID_METADEVICE = MD.ID_METADEVICE
        JOIN FS_XFILEFILM XF WITH (NOLOCK) ON XF.ID_METAFILE = MF.ID_METAFILE
        JOIN FILMATI FI WITH (NOLOCK) ON FI.ID_FILMATI = XF.ID_FILMATI
        LEFT JOIN FS_FILE FL WITH (NOLOCK) ON MF.ID_METAFILE = FL.ID_METAFILE
        LEFT JOIN FS_PATH FP WITH (NOLOCK) ON FL.ID_PATH = FP.ID_PATH
        LEFT JOIN CODECS  CO WITH (NOLOCK) ON MF.ID_CODEC = CO.ID_CODEC
 	 join codecs_prop cop1  with (nolock) on cop1.prop='proxy'
	 left join codecs_propval copv1 with (nolock) on CO.id_codec=copv1.id_codec and cop1.prop=copv1.prop
	 join codecs_prop cop2  with (nolock) on cop2.prop='lowresdef'
	 left join codecs_propval copv2 with (nolock) on CO.id_codec=copv2.id_codec and cop2.prop=copv2.prop
	 join codecs_prop cop3  with (nolock) on cop3.prop='etereplayer'
	 left join codecs_propval copv3 with (nolock) on CO.id_codec=copv3.id_codec and cop3.prop=copv3.prop

===== VIEW dbo.FS_METADEVICE_SPACE =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[FS_METADEVICE_SPACE] AS
SELECT * , 
  (SELECT cast(SUM(cast(FIL.size as decimal) / (1024*1024*1024)) as numeric(36,2)) FROM FS_FILE FIL
  
  JOIN FS_METAFILE  M ON (FIL.ID_METAFILE=M.ID_METAFILE) 
  JOIN FS_XFILEFILM X ON (X.ID_METAFILE=M.ID_METAFILE) 
  JOIN FILMATI      F ON (X.ID_FILMATI =F.ID_FILMATI) 
  WHERE M.ID_METADEVICE=V.ID_METADEVICE and
                         ((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM FUSERS U WHERE U.ID_SERIE=F.ID_SERIE)=0))  AS USED_SPACE_COMMON , 
  (SELECT cast(SUM(cast(FIL.size as decimal) / (1024*1024*1024)) as numeric(36,2)) FROM FS_FILE FIL
  JOIN FS_METAFILE  M ON (FIL.ID_METAFILE=M.ID_METAFILE) 
  JOIN FS_XFILEFILM X ON (X.ID_METAFILE=M.ID_METAFILE) 
  JOIN FILMATI      F ON (X.ID_FILMATI =F.ID_FILMATI) 
  WHERE M.ID_METADEVICE=V.ID_METADEVICE
        and ((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM FUSERS U WHERE U.ID_SERIE=F.ID_SERIE AND U.COD_USER<>V.COD_USER)=((SELECT COUNT(*)  FROM USERS)-1))) AS USED_SPACE_SINGLE
FROM FS_SPACE V

===== VIEW dbo.FS_METADEVICEPATH =====
CREATE   VIEW FS_METADEVICEPATH
AS
  SELECT 
    MD.ID_METADEVICE, 
    MD.DESCRIPTION,
    BP.ID_BASEPATH,
    BP.BASEPATH,
    BP.RS_DEVICEID,
    MD.RS_CD_MEDIA,
    FP.ID_PATH,
    FP.FULL_PATHNAME,
    MD.RS_COLOR,
    MD.ICONNAME
  FROM  FS_METADEVICE MD WITH (NOLOCK) 
        LEFT JOIN FS_BASEPATH BP WITH (NOLOCK) ON BP.ID_METADEVICE = MD.ID_METADEVICE
        LEFT JOIN FS_PATH FP WITH (NOLOCK) ON FP.ID_BASEPATH = BP.ID_BASEPATH

===== VIEW dbo.FS_METADEVICEPATH_SHARE =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[FS_METADEVICEPATH_SHARE]
AS
SELECT 
    MD.ID_METADEVICE, 
    MD.DESCRIPTION,
    BP.ID_BASEPATH,
    BP.BASEPATH,
 	r.parentId as RS_DEVICEID,
    MD.RS_CD_MEDIA,
    FP.ID_PATH,
    FP.FULL_PATHNAME,
    MD.RS_COLOR,
    MD.ICONNAME
  FROM  rs_devices r
	left join FS_BASEPATH bp on bp.ID_BASEPATH=cast(dbo.rs_getResourcePropValueXML(r.fdata,'idbasepaht1') as int) 
	left join FS_PATH fp on fp.ID_BASEPATH=bp.ID_BASEPATH
	left join FS_METADEVICE MD on MD.ID_METADEVICE=cast(dbo.rs_getResourcePropValueXML(r.fdata,'idmetadevice1') as int) 
	where r.fclass like '%.volume' and bp.RS_DEVICEID<>r.parentId

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.FS_METAFILE#FO_U#CHECK_LOGICAL_INTEGRITY =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [FS_METAFILE#FO_U#CHECK_LOGICAL_INTEGRITY] ON [FS_METAFILE]
FOR UPDATE
--NOT FOR REPLICATION
AS 
  --IF UPDATE([ID_METADEVICE]) OR UPDATE ([FILE_ID]) BEGIN
  --  RAISERROR ('Cannot modify file key values: [ID_METADEVICE] and [FILE_ID]', 16, 1)
  --  ROLLBACK TRAN
  --END ELSE 
  IF (NOT UPDATE(MODIFICATION_TIME)) AND
     (@@NESTLEVEL <= 8) BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON
    UPDATE MF WITH (ROWLOCK) 
      SET MF.MODIFICATION_TIME = GETDATE()
      FROM FS_METAFILE MF 
         JOIN INSERTED ON INSERTED.ID_METAFILE = MF.ID_METAFILE
  END

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.fs_metafile#iu#check_offline =====
CREATE   trigger [fs_metafile#iu#check_offline] on [fs_metafile]
for insert, update 
--not for replication
as 
  if update([id_metadevice]) begin
    declare @cnt int
    declare @off int
    select @cnt = count(*), @off = sum(case bp.flag_offline when 0 then 0 else 1 end)
        from fs_basepath bp with (nolock)
        join fs_metadevice md with (nolock) on bp.id_metadevice = md.id_metadevice
        join inserted i on i.id_metadevice = md.id_metadevice
    if (@cnt > 0) and (@cnt = @off)    begin  
      raiserror ('cannot link a file to an offline metadevice', 16, 1)
      rollback tran
    end
  end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.FS_PATH#AF_IU#SYNC_FULL_PATHNAME =====
CREATE TRIGGER [FS_PATH#AF_IU#SYNC_FULL_PATHNAME] ON [FS_PATH] 
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE 
NOT FOR REPLICATION
AS 
  IF UPDATE([SUBPATH]) OR UPDATE([ID_BASEPATH]) BEGIN
    UPDATE P WITH (ROWLOCK) 
      SET P.[FULL_PATHNAME] = [dbo].[fs_getFullPathname](I.ID_PATH)
      FROM [FS_PATH] P 
         JOIN INSERTED I ON P.ID_PATH = I.ID_PATH
  END

===== VIEW dbo.fs_sl_devCodecGroups =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.fs_sl_devCodecGroups
    -- reports all group of codecs for each metadevice
    -- Given a ceratin metadevice, if ID_CODEC_1 is considered as the 
    -- base codec then all row that has same metadev and codec_1 but
    -- different codec_2 are grouped together: that means that if you
    -- create a metafile of codec_1 on that given metadevice then also 
    -- metafile of codec_2 must be created too
    as
        select 
            bp.ID_METADEVICE as ID_METADEVICE, 
            xs.ID_CODEC as ID_CODEC_1, 
            isnull(cg.id_codec, xs.ID_CODEC) as ID_CODEC_2,
            cg.id_codecgroup as ID_CODECGROUP
        from fs_basepath bp with (nolock) 
            join fs_xPathStorage xs with (nolock) on xs.ID_BASEPATH = bp.ID_BASEPATH
            join fs_storageLayout sl with (nolock) on sl.ID_STORAGELAYOUT = xs.ID_STORAGELAYOUT
            join fs_metadevice md with (nolock) on md.ID_METADEVICE = bp.ID_METADEVICE
            join codecs cd with (nolock) on cd.ID_CODEC = xs.ID_CODEC
            left join fs_xPathStorage cg with (nolock) on xs.ID_CODECGROUP = cg.ID_CODECGROUP and xs.fileexplode = 1 
        group by bp.ID_METADEVICE, xs.ID_CODEC, cg.id_codecgroup, cg.id_codec

===== VIEW dbo.fs_sl_metafilePhysExpansion =====
CREATE   view dbo.fs_sl_metafilePhysExpansion
as 
        -- sl rule expansion: this is the 'theorical' physical layout of
        -- files given the storage layout config... each ID_METAFILE has
        -- his associated physical files ID_PATH \ [FILE_NAME]
        select
            mf.id_metafile as ID_METAFILE,
            fp.id_path ID_PATH, 
            phyf.[file_name] AS [FILE_NAME]
        from fs_metafile mf
            join fs_basepath bp with (nolock) on bp.ID_METADEVICE = mf.ID_METADEVICE
            join fs_xPathStorage xs with (nolock) on xs.ID_BASEPATH = bp.ID_BASEPATH and xs.ID_CODEC = mf.ID_CODEC
            left join fs_storageLayout sl with (nolock) on sl.ID_STORAGELAYOUT = xs.ID_STORAGELAYOUT
            outer apply dbo.fs_sl_expandFiles(sl.XML_LAYOUT,mf.[file_id]) phyf
            join fs_path fp with (nolock) on fp.ID_BASEPATH = bp.ID_BASEPATH and fp.SUBPATH = phyf.subdir
        group by mf.id_metafile, fp.id_path, phyf.[file_name]

===== VIEW dbo.FS_VWFILES =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[FS_VWFILES]
AS
select 
	id_filmati,
	m.id_metafile,
	m.id_metadevice,
	m.file_id,
	m.id_codec,
	m.flag_offline,
	c.type,
	isnull(copv1.value,cop1.defaultvalue) as proxy,
	isnull(copv2.value,cop2.defaultvalue) as lowresdef,
	p.full_pathname,
	f.file_name,
 	f.id_path,
	d.rs_cd_media
	from fs_xfilefilm  x  with (nolock) 
	    join fs_metafile   m  with (nolock) on x.id_metafile=m.id_metafile
	    join codecs        c  with (nolock) on m.id_codec=c.id_codec
	    join fs_file       f  with (nolock) on m.id_metafile=f.id_metafile
	    join fs_path       p  with (nolock) on f.id_path=p.id_path
	    join fs_metadevice d  with (nolock) on m.id_metadevice=d.id_metadevice and rs_cd_media <> 'hsm' 
		join codecs_prop cop1  with (nolock) on cop1.prop='proxy'
		left join codecs_propval copv1 with (nolock) on c.id_codec=copv1.id_codec and cop1.prop=copv1.prop
		join codecs_prop cop2  with (nolock) on cop2.prop='lowresdef'
		left join codecs_propval copv2 with (nolock) on c.id_codec=copv2.id_codec and cop2.prop=copv2.prop

===== VIEW dbo.FS_VWFLOWRESFILES =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[FS_VWFLOWRESFILES]
AS
select 
	id_filmati,
	m.id_metafile,
	m.id_metadevice,
	m.file_id,
	m.id_codec,
	m.flag_offline,
	c.type,
	isnull(copv2.value,cop2.defaultvalue) as lowresdef,
	p.full_pathname, 
	f.file_name,
 	f.id_path,
	d.rs_cd_media,
	f.ID_FILE,
	c.VideoStd
	from fs_xfilefilm  x  with (nolock) 
	    join fs_metafile   m  with (nolock) on x.id_metafile=m.id_metafile
	    join codecs        c  with (nolock) on m.id_codec=c.id_codec
	    join codecs_prop cop1  with (nolock) on cop1.prop='proxy'
	    join codecs_propval copv1 with (nolock) on c.id_codec=copv1.id_codec and cop1.prop=copv1.prop
	    join fs_file       f  with (nolock) on m.id_metafile=f.id_metafile
	    join fs_path       p  with (nolock) on f.id_path=p.id_path
	    join fs_metadevice d  with (nolock) on m.id_metadevice=d.id_metadevice and rs_cd_media <> 'hsm'
	    join codecs_prop cop2  with (nolock) on cop2.prop='lowresdef'
	    left join codecs_propval copv2 with (nolock) on c.id_codec=copv2.id_codec and cop2.prop=copv2.prop

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.Fs_xfilefilmUpdateEdlChecksum =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[Fs_xfilefilmUpdateEdlChecksum] ON [dbo].[fedldescription]
FOR INSERT,UPDATE
AS
begin
	if	(update (schedule_checksum)) and 
		(-1 <> (select top 1 schedule_checksum from inserted))
	begin
		declare @chk int
		select @chk = dbo.GetXFileFilmEdlCheckSum(id_filmati) from Inserted
		
		update F with (rowlock) set
		EDLCHECKSUM = @chk,
		EDLCHECKSTATUS = case when EDLCHECKSTATUS is NULL then NULL else 0 end 
		from Fs_xfilefilm F
		join Inserted I on I.ID_Filmati = F.ID_Filmati 
		where isnull(EDLCHECKSUM,0) <> @chk		
	
	end
end

===== VIEW dbo.getProp_RaggruppaInCluster =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[getProp_RaggruppaInCluster]
AS
SELECT     t.ID_TPALINSE,t.cod_user,t.data
FROM         dbo.tpalinse t LEFT OUTER JOIN
             dbo.tipologieprop p ON p.COD_TYPE = t.NEWTYPE
WHERE     (p.PROP = 'oiRaggruppaInCluster')

===== VIEW dbo.hsm_mp_realign_summary =====
CREATE   view dbo.hsm_mp_realign_summary
as
-- sumary by metafile archived in not expected mediapools and/or having missing copies --
	select v.id_metafile, v.file_id, v.id_codec, v.id_metadevice, v.id_filmati, v.cod_progra, v.newtype
	, unexptected_id_metadevice=max(v.unexptected_id_metadevice), missing_copies=count(v.missing_copynum)
	from (
		select id_metafile, file_id, id_codec, id_metadevice, id_filmati, cod_progra, newtype
		, unexptected_id_metadevice=id_metadevice, missing_copynum=null
		from dbo.hsm_mp_realignview		-- metafiles archived in not expected hsm mediapools --
		union
		select id_metafile, file_id, id_codec, id_metadevice, id_filmati, cod_progra, newtype
		, unexptected_id_metadevice=null, missing_copynum=isnull(copynum,1)
		from hsm_mp_realigncopiesview		-- missing copies of hsm archived metafiles --
	) v
	group by v.file_id, v.id_codec, v.id_metadevice, v.id_metafile, v.id_filmati, v.cod_progra, v.newtype

===== VIEW dbo.hsm_mp_realign_summarytodo =====
CREATE   view dbo.hsm_mp_realign_summarytodo
as
	SELECT mfs.*, arcsrc_id_metafile=arcsrc.id_metafile
	, CASE WHEN mfs.missing_copies > 0 THEN                   --Metafile has MISSING COPIES--
		CASE WHEN arcsrc.id_metafile > 0 THEN                 ----Metafile has copies on DISK--
		  CASE WHEN mfs.unexptected_id_metadevice > 0 THEN        
			'AX'    --cast(mfs.missing_copies as varchar) + ' copy/copies missed. Must be REARCHIVED from disk and then DELETED from this unexpected mediapool.'
		  ELSE                                                     
			'A'     --cast(mfs.missing_copies as varchar) + ' copy/copies missed. Must be REARCHIVED from disk.'
		  END
		ELSE                                                  ----Metafile has NO copies on DISK--
		  CASE WHEN mfs.unexptected_id_metadevice > 0 THEN        
			'RAX'    --cast(mfs.missing_copies as varchar) + ' copy/copies missed. Must be RESTORED and REARCHIVED and then DELETED from this unexpected mediapool.'
		  ELSE                                                    
			'RA'     --cast(mfs.missing_copies as varchar) + ' copy/copies missed. Must be RESTORED and REARCHIVED.'
		  END
		END
	  ELSE                                                    --Metafile has NO MISSING COPIES--
	   CASE WHEN mfs.unexptected_id_metadevice > 0 THEN       ----Metafile is in UNEXPECTED mediapool--
		 'X'         --'must be DELETED from this unexpected mediapool (all needed copies are archived in HSM).' 
	   END
	  END AS todo
	FROM dbo.hsm_mp_realign_summary mfs WITH(NOLOCK)
	OUTER APPLY (  -- Copy on Disk: 
	  SELECT TOP 1 mf1.id_metafile 
	  FROM fs_metafile mf1 WITH(NOLOCK) 
	  LEFT JOIN fs_metadevice md1 WITH(NOLOCK) ON md1.id_metadevice=mf1.id_metadevice 
	  WHERE mf1.file_id=mfs.file_id AND mf1.id_codec=mfs.id_codec 
	  AND dbo.hsm_IsArchSourceMf(mf1.id_metafile)=1 
	  AND ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL1', mf1.id_metafile), 0) = ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL1', mfs.id_metafile), 0)
	  AND ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL2', mf1.id_metafile), 0) = ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL2', mfs.id_metafile), 0)
	  AND ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL3', mf1.id_metafile), 0) = ISNULL(dbo.smpte_GetMapIntFieldMF('FILEINFO', 'HSMARCHIVEMEDIAPOOL3', mfs.id_metafile), 0)
	  ORDER BY CASE md1.rs_cd_media WHEN 'hsm.cache' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END 
	) arcsrc

===== VIEW dbo.hsm_mp_realigncopiesview =====
CREATE   view dbo.hsm_mp_realigncopiesview
as
-- missing copies of hsm archived metafiles --
	SELECT mf.id_metafile, mf.file_id, mf.id_codec, mf.id_metadevice, f.id_filmati, f.cod_progra, f.newtype, mp.copynum, mp.dest_id_mediapool
	FROM fs_metafile mf WITH(NOLOCK)
	JOIN fs_xfilefilm xf WITH(NOLOCK) ON xf.id_metafile=mf.id_metafile
	JOIN filmati f WITH(NOLOCK) ON f.id_filmati=xf.id_filmati
	OUTER APPLY (						-- list of required destination mediapools
		SELECT copynum, mediapool_id AS dest_id_mediapool FROM dbo.hsm_mp_getMediaPools(mf.id_metafile, f.newtype, mf.id_codec)
		--SELECT tymp.copynum, dbo.hsm_mp_getMediaPool(tymp.value, tymp.copynum, null, mf.id_codec) AS dest_id_mediapool
		--FROM ( 
		--	SELECT te.value, pccn.copynum
		--	FROM tipologie t WITH(NOLOCK)
		--	LEFT JOIN tipologie_ext te WITH(NOLOCK) ON te.cod_par='HSMP' AND te.cod_type=t.cod_type 
		--	OUTER APPLY (SELECT DISTINCT copynum FROM hsm_poolcopy WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE CAST(id_pool AS varchar)=te.value) pccn
		--	WHERE t.cod_type=f.newtype 
		--) tymp
	) mp
	JOIN fs_metadevice md WITH(NOLOCK) ON md.id_metadevice=mf.id_metadevice
	LEFT JOIN fs_metafile mfx WITH(NOLOCK) ON mfx.file_id=mf.file_id AND mfx.id_codec=mf.id_codec AND mfx.id_metadevice=mp.dest_id_mediapool	--copy in required destination mediapool
	WHERE md.rs_cd_media='hsm'				-- metafiles archived in hsm
	AND mfx.id_metafile IS NULL				-- copy does not exist in required destination mediapool

===== VIEW dbo.hsm_mp_realignview =====
CREATE   view dbo.hsm_mp_realignview
as
-- metafiles archived in not expected hsm mediapools --
	SELECT mf.id_metafile, mf.file_id, mf.id_codec, f.id_filmati, f.cod_progra, f.newtype
	, md.id_metadevice, mediapool=md.description
	FROM fs_metafile mf WITH(NOLOCK)
	JOIN fs_xfilefilm xf WITH(NOLOCK) ON xf.id_metafile=mf.id_metafile
	JOIN filmati f WITH(NOLOCK) ON f.id_filmati=xf.id_filmati
	JOIN fs_metadevice md WITH(NOLOCK) ON md.id_metadevice=mf.id_metadevice
	WHERE md.rs_cd_media='hsm'		-- metafiles archived in hsm
	AND md.id_metadevice NOT IN (		-- archived in a mediapool that is not a mediapool for the asset type
		SELECT mediapool_id FROM dbo.hsm_mp_getMediaPools(mf.id_metafile, f.newtype, mf.id_codec)
		--SELECT dbo.hsm_mp_getMediaPool(tymp.value, tymp.copynum, null, mf.id_codec)
		--FROM ( 
		--	SELECT te.value, pccn.copynum
		--	FROM tipologie t WITH(NOLOCK)
		--	LEFT JOIN tipologie_ext te WITH(NOLOCK) ON te.cod_par='HSMP' AND te.cod_type=t.cod_type 
		--	OUTER APPLY (SELECT DISTINCT copynum FROM hsm_poolcopy WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE CAST(id_pool AS varchar)=te.value) pccn
		--	WHERE t.cod_type=f.newtype
		--) tymp
	)

===== VIEW dbo.hsm_mp_realignviewh2 =====
CREATE   view dbo.hsm_mp_realignviewh2
as
	SELECT hf.id_hsmfile, hf.file_name, bp.ID_METADEVICE, hf.id_supporti, hf.cod_user 
	FROM (
		SELECT id_hsmfile, file_name, id_supporti, cod_user = CAST(SUBSTRING(file_name, 4, 3) AS int)
		FROM hsm_file WITH(NOLOCK)
		WHERE id_file = 0 AND custom_use = 2	-- hsm custom files: memory files archive
	) hf
	JOIN fsupporti fs WITH(NOLOCK) ON fs.id_supporti=hf.id_supporti
	JOIN fs_basepath bp WITH(NOLOCK) ON bp.basepath=dbo.fs_hsmBarcodeToPath(fs.barcode)
	OUTER APPLY (
		SELECT TOP 1 id_pool = CAST(obj_value AS varchar)
		FROM inifiles WITH(NOLOCK) 
		WHERE obj_name IN (N'global.ini/Etere HSM Headquarters/MemoryBkpPoolsId') 
		AND cod_user IS NULL AND pc_name IS NULL AND login_name IS NULL 
		ORDER BY lastmodified 
	) ini
	WHERE bp.id_metadevice NOT IN (		-- archived in a mediapool that is not a mediapool for the cod_user
		SELECT dbo.hsm_mp_getMediaPool(ini.id_pool, tymp.copynum, hf.cod_user, 0)
		FROM (SELECT DISTINCT copynum FROM hsm_poolcopy WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE id_pool=ini.id_pool) tymp
	)
	AND bp.id_metadevice <> (			-- archived in a mediapool that is not 'No Media Pool', whenever cod_user has no mediapool setted and then follows the default 1 copy in 'No Media Pool'
		SELECT
		CASE WHEN NOT EXISTS (
			SELECT 1 FROM hsm_poolcopy WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE id_pool=ini.id_pool AND cod_user=hf.cod_user
		) THEN
			(SELECT id_metadevice FROM fs_metadevice WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE rs_cd_media='hsm' AND description='No Media Pool')
		ELSE
			0
		END 
	)

===== VIEW dbo.hsmCassette =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[hsmCassette]
AS
  select fs.id_supporti, fs.barcode, fs.free, fs.expired, st.supp_type, suppCapacity=st.capacity, specCapacity=fs.capacity, Capacity=ISNULL(fs.capacity,st.capacity)--capacity=st.capacity, 
  , DataFormat = case when fs.free=0 then isnull(fs.dataformat,'EXF') else null end
  , fs.last_write, fs.last_read, fs.data_con  --new date&time'uses fields
  , fs.readonly, fs.unusable, fs.dataerror
  from fsupporti fs with(nolock)
  left join fsupp_types st with(nolock) on st.supp_type=rtrim(substring(fs.supporto,6,5))
  where st.supporttype=2

===== VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteLocation =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteLocation
AS
	SELECT 
	  hc.id_supporti, hc.barcode, hc.free, hc.expired, hc.supp_type, hc.DataFormat, hc.readonly, hc.unusable, hc.dataerror
	, location = CASE WHEN d.id_drives IS NOT NULL THEN 1 WHEN s.riga >= 0 THEN 0 WHEN s.riga = -50 THEN 50 ELSE 99 END 
	, number = CASE WHEN d.id_drives IS NOT NULL THEN d.Ndrives WHEN s.ID_slots IS NOT NULL THEN s.Nslot ELSE NULL END 
	, rackname = r.nome
	, r.id_racks, s.id_slots, d.id_drives
	, LastWrite=hc.last_write, LastRead=hc.last_read, LastUse=hc.data_con  --new date&time'uses fields
	FROM dbo.hsmCassette hc
	JOIN fsupporti fs WITH(NOLOCK) ON fs.id_supporti=hc.id_supporti
	LEFT JOIN slots s WITH(NOLOCK) ON s.id_slots=fs.slot
	LEFT JOIN drives d WITH(NOLOCK) ON d.id_drives=s.id_drives
	LEFT JOIN racks r WITH(NOLOCK) ON r.id_racks=s.id_racks

===== VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteSpace =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteSpace
AS
	SELECT hc.id_supporti, hc.barcode, hc.free, hc.expired, hc.supp_type, hc.readonly, hc.unusable, hc.dataerror, hc.DataFormat, hc.suppCapacity AS SuppCapacity,--hc.capacity AS SuppCapacity, 
		--CASE WHEN ISNULL(fss.FilesCount, 0) > 0 THEN ISNULL(fss.FilesCount, 0) ELSE ISNULL(ltfs.FilesCount, 0) END AS FilesCount, 
		ISNULL(fss.FilesCount, 0) AS FilesCount, 
		--ISNULL(fss.UsedSpace, ltfs.UsedSpace) AS UsedSpace,
		--ISNULL(fss.DeletedSpace, ltfs.DeletedSpace) AS DeletedSpace,
		fss.UsedSpace, fss.DeletedSpace,
		ISNULL(hft.remaining, hc.Capacity) AS FreeSpace,
		--CASE WHEN (ISNULL(hft.remaining, hc.capacity) + ISNULL(fss.UsedSpace, ltfs.UsedSpace)) = 0 THEN NULL ELSE CAST(ISNULL(fss.DeletedSpace, ltfs.DeletedSpace) * 100 AS float) / (ISNULL(hft.remaining, hc.capacity) + ISNULL(fss.UsedSpace, ltfs.UsedSpace)) END AS DeletedPerc,
		CASE WHEN (ISNULL(hft.Remaining, hc.capacity) + fss.UsedSpace) = 0 THEN NULL ELSE CAST(DeletedSpace * 100 AS float) / (ISNULL(hft.Remaining, hc.capacity) + fss.UsedSpace) END AS DeletedPerc, 
		CASE WHEN hft.remaining IS NULL THEN hc.capacity ELSE hft.remaining + ISNULL(fss.UsedSpace, 0) END AS TapeCapacity
	FROM dbo.hsmCassette hc
	OUTER APPLY (
		SELECT 
			COUNT(id_hsmfile) AS FilesCount, 
			SUM(file_size) AS UsedSpace,
			SUM(CASE WHEN id_file IS NULL THEN file_size ELSE 0 END) AS DeletedSpace
		FROM hsm_file hf WITH(NOLOCK)
		WHERE hf.id_supporti=hc.id_supporti
	) AS fss 
	--OUTER APPLY  (
	--	SELECT 
	--		COUNT(ff.id_file) AS FilesCount, 
	--		SUM(ff.size) as UsedSpace,
	--		NULL AS DeletedSpace
	--	FROM fs_path fp WITH(NOLOCK) 
	--	JOIN fs_file ff  WITH(NOLOCK) ON ff.id_path=fp.id_path
	--	WHERE fp.full_pathname=dbo.fs_hsmBarcodeToPath(hc.barcode)
	--) AS ltfs 
	OUTER APPLY (
		SELECT TOP 1 remaining
		FROM hsm_file WITH(NOLOCK) 
		WHERE id_supporti=hc.id_supporti
		ORDER BY iniblock DESC, remaining ASC
	) hft

===== VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteSpaceBooked =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteSpaceBooked
AS
	select hcp.id_supporti, hcp.barcode, hcp.free, hcp.expired, hcp.supp_type, hcp.readonly, hcp.unusable, hcp.dataerror, hcp.DataFormat, hcp.SuppCapacity
	, hcp.FilesCount, hcp.UsedSpace, hcp.DeletedSpace, hcp.FreeSpace, hcp.DeletedPerc, hcp.TapeCapacity
	, wq.BookedSpace, FreeUnbookedSpace = (hcp.FreeSpace - wq.BookedSpace)
	from dbo.hsmCassetteSpace hcp
	outer apply (
	  select BookedSpace=isnull(sum(filesize), 0)
	  from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	  where queued>0 and terminated=0 and expired=0 
	  and optype in ('Backup','Defrag','MigrateTo') 
	  and medianame=hcp.barcode 
	) wq

===== VIEW dbo.hsmCassetteUse =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[hsmCassetteUse] --only for backward compatibility after adding of new date&time'uses fields
AS
  select  
    hc.id_supporti, hc.barcode, hc.free, hc.expired, hc.supp_type,
  --LastWrite=(
  -- SELECT MAX (CASE endtime WHEN 0 THEN starttime ELSE endtime END) FROM hsmhistory WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE medianame=hc.barcode AND optype='Backup'
  --), 
  --LastRead=(
  -- SELECT MAX (CASE endtime WHEN 0 THEN starttime ELSE endtime END) FROM hsmhistory WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE medianame=hc.barcode AND optype='Restore'
  --), 
  --LastUse=(
  -- SELECT MAX (CASE endtime WHEN 0 THEN starttime ELSE endtime END) FROM hsmhistory WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE medianame=hc.barcode 
  --) 
    LastWrite=hc.last_write, LastRead=hc.last_read, LastUse=hc.data_con  --new date&time'uses fields
  from dbo.hsmCassette hc

===== VIEW dbo.hsmDevices =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.hsmDevices
AS      
	SELECT dv.deviceid, dv.name
	, parms.ServerName, parms.IP, parms.Port
	, parms.Server2Name, parms.Server2IP, parms.Server2Port
	, CAST(dv.design AS xml).value('(/reserved/@devClassId)[1]', 'int' ) AS DevClassId
	FROM (
	  SELECT deviceid, name, design, CAST(('<a>'+fdata+'</a>') AS xml) AS xmlfdata FROM rs_devices WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE fclass='hsm' 
	) dv 
	OUTER APPLY (
	  SELECT n.c.value('@serverName', 'nvarchar(max)') AS ServerName, n.c.value('@ip', 'varchar(15)') AS IP, n.c.value('@port', 'int') AS Port 
	  , n.c.value('@server2Name', 'nvarchar(max)') AS Server2Name, n.c.value('@server2ip', 'varchar(15)') AS Server2IP, n.c.value('@server2port', 'int') AS Server2Port
	  FROM dv.xmlfdata.nodes('a/param') n(c) 
	) parms

===== VIEW dbo.hsmErrors =====
CREATE   view [dbo].[hsmErrors]
as
select 
	optype, file_id, id_codec, id_filmati, hsmerrdt.medianame, filename,
	id_hsmworkqueue, requested, queued, [message], drivename, libraryname, server 
from (
	-- operazioni METAFILE in errore nella coda lavori hsm -- 
	select opon='metafile', optype, file_id, id_codec, id_filmati, medianame=null, filename=null 
	from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	where termination_flag='E' and terminated>0 
	and optype in ('Backup', 'Restore')
	group by optype, id_filmati, file_id, id_codec
	union
	-- operazioni TAPE in errore nella coda lavori hsm -- 
	select opon='tape', optype, file_id=null, id_codec=null, id_filmati=null, medianame, filename=null
	from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	where termination_flag='E' and terminated>0 
	and optype not in ('Backup', 'Restore')
	group by optype, medianame
	union
	-- archiviazioni CUSTOM in errore nella coda lavori hsm -- 
	select opon='custom', optype, file_id=null, id_codec=null, id_filmati=null, medianame=null, filename
	from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	where termination_flag='E' and terminated>0 
	and optype in ('Backup') and options like '%H%'
	group by optype, filename
) as hsmerr
outer apply (
	-- METAFILE relativi alle operazioni in errore --
	select mf.id_metafile
	from fs_metafile mf with(nolock)
	join fs_metadevice md with(nolock) on md.id_metadevice=mf.id_metadevice 
	where hsmerr.opon='metafile' and mf.file_id=hsmerr.file_id and mf.id_codec=hsmerr.id_codec
	and (
	  (hsmerr.optype='Backup' and md.rs_cd_media='hsm') or
	  (hsmerr.optype='Restore' and  md.rs_cd_media<>'hsm')
	)
) as mfexists
outer apply (
	-- TAPE relativi alle operazioni in errore --
	select top 1 medianame, termination_flag
	from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	where hsmerr.opon='tape' and medianame=hsmerr.medianame
	and optype=hsmerr.optype and terminated>0 
	order by terminated desc
) as tapelast
outer apply (
	-- CUSTOM FILE relativi alle operazioni in errore --
	select top 1 hf.file_name
	from hsm_file hf with(nolock)
	where hsmerr.opon='custom' and hf.file_name=hsmerr.filename
) as cfexists
cross apply (
    -- dettaglio ultima operazione in errore --
	select top 1 id_hsmworkqueue, requested, queued, [message], medianame, drivename, libraryname, server
	from hsmworkqueue with(nolock)
	where optype=hsmerr.optype 
	and (
		(hsmerr.opon='metafile' and file_id=hsmerr.file_id and id_codec=hsmerr.id_codec) 
		or (hsmerr.opon='tape' and medianame=hsmerr.medianame)
		or (hsmerr.opon='custom' and filename=hsmerr.filename)
	)
	and termination_flag='E' and terminated>0 
	order by id_hsmworkqueue desc
) as hsmerrdt
where (hsmerr.opon='metafile' and mfexists.id_metafile is null)		-- visualizza le operazioni: -backup con metafile non archiviato, -restore con metafile non restorato.
or (hsmerr.opon='tape' and isnull(tapelast.termination_flag,'')='E')	-- visualizza le operazioni: -tape con ultima operazione in errore.
or (hsmerr.opon='custom' and cfexists.file_name is null)	-- visualizza le operazioni: -custom backup con file non archiviato.

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.INIFILES_LASTMODIFIED =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.INIFILES_LASTMODIFIED
ON dbo.INIFILES
FOR UPDATE
--NOT FOR REPLICATION
AS
  SET NOCOUNT ON
  UPDATE INIFILES 
  SET INIFILES.LASTMODIFIED = GETDATE()
  FROM INIFILES 
    JOIN INSERTED ON INSERTED.ID_INIFILES = INIFILES.ID_INIFILES

===== VIEW dbo.languages =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[languages]
AS
	select l.name, l.alias, l.lcid, 
		CASE WHEN el.lcid IS NULL THEN NULL ELSE 1 END AS IsEtLang,
		l.Dictionary_Dic, l.Dictionary_Aff, l.bcp47, l.MSSpeechRecognizerID, l.iso_639_2, l.iso_639_1, l.reverse, l.TesseractOCR, l.Google_Code 
	from env_language l
	left join etLang el on l.lcid=el.lcid
	/*
	select l.name, l.alias, l.lcid, 
	    CASE WHEN (SELECT TOP 1 el.lcid FROM etlang el WITH(NOLOCK) WHERE el.lcid=l.lcid) IS NULL THEN NULL ELSE 1 END AS IsEtLang
	from (
		SELECT name, alias, lcid  FROM sys.syslanguages
		union
		select	'Vietnamese', 'Vietnamese', 1066
		union
		select	'Bahasa Indonesia','Bahasa Indonesia', 1057
		union
		select	'Bahasa Malaysia','Bahasa Malaysia', 1086
		) l
	*/

===== VIEW dbo.lock_view =====
CREATE   view lock_view
as
  select 
    l.[id_object],
    o.[lock_mode],
    l.[object_name],
    l.[object_id],
    l.[object_key],
    o.[owner_name],
    o.[owner_id],
    o.[owner_key],
    o.[os_login],
    o.[hostname],
    o.[program_name],
    o.[hostprocess],
    o.[timestamp],
    l.[ref_count],
    l.[n_acquire],
    l.[n_release],
    l.[n_granted],
    l.[n_rejected],
    l.[checkmark]
  from 
    lock_object l with (nolock) 
      join lock_owner o with (nolock) on o.id_object = l.id_object

===== VIEW dbo.mem_cfgMachines =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.mem_cfgMachines
AS
  select *
  , MainBackup=case dbo.mem_cfgLoadStr(MachineName, cod_user, instance, 'GENERALI', 'avviobackup', '0') when '1' then 'B' else 'M' end
  from (
	select distinct MachineName=pc_name, cod_user
	, instance=substring(obj_name, charindex('.', obj_name, charindex('.ini/Memory', obj_name)+11)+1, 1)
	--, obj_name, obj_value=cast(obj_value as nvarchar(max))	
	from inifiles where obj_name like '%.ini/Memory%\ETX/XmlPropsCount'
  ) c

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.memory_job_creation_time =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[memory_job_creation_time] ON [dbo].[memory_job]
FOR INSERT 
AS
begin
	if (not update(creation_time) or ((select top 1 creation_time from inserted) is null))
	begin
		declare @count int
		select @count = count(*) from inserted
		if @count>0
		begin
			declare @id_memory_job bigint
			declare id_memory_job_changed cursor for select id_memory_job from inserted
			open id_memory_job_changed
			fetch next from id_memory_job_changed into @id_memory_job
			while @@fetch_status=0
			begin
				update memory_job set creation_time=getutcdate() where id_memory_job=@id_memory_job
	
				fetch next from id_memory_job_changed into @id_memory_job
			end
			close id_memory_job_changed
			deallocate id_memory_job_changed
		end
	end
	
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.memory_list_lastupdate =====
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[memory_list_lastupdate] ON [dbo].[memory_list]
FOR INSERT, UPDATE 
AS
begin
	if (not update(lastupdate) or ((select top 1 lastupdate from inserted) is null))
	begin
		declare @count int
		select @count = count(*) from inserted
		if @count>0
		begin
			declare @id_memory_list bigint
			declare id_memory_list_changed cursor for select id_memory_list from inserted
			open id_memory_list_changed
			fetch next from id_memory_list_changed into @id_memory_list
			while @@fetch_status=0
			begin
				update memory_list set lastupdate=getutcdate() where id_memory_list=@id_memory_list
	
				fetch next from id_memory_list_changed into @id_memory_list
			end
			close id_memory_list_changed
			deallocate id_memory_list_changed
		end
	end
	
end

===== VIEW dbo.mtx_IngestProfiles =====
CREATE   view [dbo].[mtx_IngestProfiles]
as
        select t.[id], t.[supported_board], t.[caption], t.[description], 
               isnull(t.[id_codec], c.ID_CODEC) as ID_CODEC, t.[dur_max]
        from [dbo].[mtx_cfg_template] t with(nolock)
          left join [dbo].[codecs] c with(nolock) on c.type = t.[default_codec_type]
        where [template_type] = 'sw' and [service_type] = 'ingest'

===== VIEW dbo.nz_feed_view =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.nz_feed_view
AS
	SELECT assetID=fi.id_filmati, AssetCode=fi.cod_progra, AssetType=fi.newtype
	, title=fi.descrizio, description=fi.trama, pub_date=fi.data_prod, rec_date=fi.data_arrivo  --, pub_date=dbo.UtcMan_UTCToLocal(f.pub_date), rec_date=dbo.UtcMan_UTCToLocal(f.rec_date)
	, f.id_feed, f.link, f.mod_date, f.id_subscription
	, sv.id_agency, sv.agency
	, sv.categories
	FROM filmati fi WITH(NOLOCK)
	JOIN nz_feed f WITH(NOLOCK) ON f.id_feed=fi.id_feed 
	JOIN nz_subscription_view sv WITH(NOLOCK) ON sv.id_subscription=f.id_subscription

===== VIEW dbo.nz_feedmedia_view =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.nz_feedmedia_view
AS
	SELECT assetID=fi.id_filmati, f.id_feed
	, fp.full_pathname, ff.file_name, ff.size, mf.id_metafile, mf.file_id, mf.som, mf.dur, mf.id_metadevice, mf.id_codec
	, Metadevice=md.description, MetadeviceIcon=md.iconname
	, Codec=co.type, CodecIcon=co.icon
	, Previewable = CASE WHEN fp.full_pathname LIKE '\\%' OR fp.full_pathname LIKE '_:\%' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
	FROM filmati fi WITH(NOLOCK)
	JOIN nz_feed f WITH(NOLOCK) ON f.id_feed=fi.id_feed 
	JOIN fs_xfilefilm xf WITH(NOLOCK) ON xf.id_filmati=fi.id_filmati
	JOIN fs_metafile mf WITH(NOLOCK) ON mf.id_metafile=xf.id_metafile
	JOIN fs_file ff WITH(NOLOCK) ON ff.id_metafile=mf.id_metafile
	JOIN fs_path fp WITH(NOLOCK) ON fp.id_path=ff.id_path
	LEFT JOIN codecs co WITH(NOLOCK) ON co.id_codec=mf.id_codec
	LEFT JOIN fs_metadevice md WITH(NOLOCK) ON md.id_metadevice=mf.id_metadevice

===== VIEW dbo.nz_subscription_view =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.nz_subscription_view
AS
	SELECT s.id_subscription, s.url, s.sourcetype, s.enabled, s.id_agency
	, agency=a.rag_social
	, scs.categories
	, id_metadeviceto=s.id_metadevice
	, s.createstory
	, s.textfile_writeto, s.textfile_maxrows
	FROM nz_subscription s WITH(NOLOCK) 
	JOIN anagraf a WITH(NOLOCK) ON a.id_anagraf=s.id_agency  
	CROSS APPLY (  
		SELECT categories = (  
			SELECT (' ['+c.name +'] ')  
			FROM nz_subscriptioncategory sc WITH(NOLOCK)   
			JOIN nz_category c WITH(NOLOCK) ON c.id_category=sc.id_category  
			WHERE sc.id_subscription=s.id_subscription   
			ORDER BY c.name  
			FOR XML PATH(''), TYPE  
		).value('data(.)', 'nvarchar(max)')  
	) scs

===== VIEW dbo.nz_subscriptioncategory_view =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.nz_subscriptioncategory_view
AS
	  SELECT id_agency=a.id_anagraf, agency=a.rag_social, c.id_category, category=c.name, s.id_subscription, s.url  
      FROM anagraf a WITH(NOLOCK)  
      JOIN nz_subscription s WITH(NOLOCK) ON s.id_agency=a.id_anagraf  
      JOIN nz_subscriptioncategory sc WITH(NOLOCK) ON sc.id_subscription=s.id_subscription  
      JOIN nz_category c WITH(NOLOCK) ON c.id_category=sc.id_category

===== VIEW dbo.pm_cfgView =====
CREATE   view dbo.pm_cfgView
as 
        select 
            cfg.id_config,
            cfg.name,
            cfg.cod_user,
            cfg.data,
            params.N_TILES,
            params.N_QUEUED,
            params.AUDIO_FADEIN,
            params.AUDIO_FADEOUT,
            params.AUDIO_CROSSP,
            params.AUDIO_DBIN,
            params.AUDIO_DBOUT
        from pm_config cfg with (nolock)
            outer apply (
                select 
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="r.ntiles"][1]/@value', 'int') as N_TILES,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="r.nqueued"][1]/@value', 'int') as N_QUEUED,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="a.fadein"][1]/@value', 'int') as AUDIO_FADEIN,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="a.fadeout"][1]/@value', 'int') as AUDIO_FADEOUT,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="a.crossp"][1]/@value', 'int') as AUDIO_CROSSP,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="a.dbin"][1]/@value', 'int') as AUDIO_DBIN,
                    n.c.value('./param[@name="a.dbout"][1]/@value', 'int') as AUDIO_DBOUT
                from cfg.data.nodes('config') n(c)  
            ) params

===== VIEW dbo.primary_keys =====
CREATE   view dbo.primary_keys as
  select distinct 
    tbl.name TableName, 
    constrId.name PkName, 
    col.name ColName, 
    sik.keyno,
    case when ix.indid = 1 then 1 else 0 end IsClustered,
    scm.name SchemaName
  from sysobjects tbl 
	join sys.schemas scm on tbl.uid =scm.schema_id
    join sysconstraints constr on ( tbl.id = constr.id and tbl.xtype = 'U' and constr.status & 0x0001 = 0x0001 )
    join sysobjects constrId on constrId.parent_obj = tbl.id and constrId.xtype = 'PK'
    join sysindexes ix on constrId.name = ix.name and ix.id = tbl.id
    join sysindexkeys sik on sik.id = tbl.id and sik.indid = ix.indid
    join syscolumns col on col.id = tbl.id and sik.colid = col.colid
/* babelfish version also valid for MS SQL **
SELECT DISTINCT
    t.name AS TableName,
    kc.name AS PkName,
    c.name AS ColName,
    ic.key_ordinal AS keyno,
    CASE WHEN i.type = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsClustered,
    s.name AS SchemaName
FROM sys.tables t
JOIN sys.schemas s
    ON t.schema_id = s.schema_id
JOIN sys.key_constraints kc
    ON kc.parent_object_id = t.object_id
   AND kc.type = 'PK'
JOIN sys.indexes i
    ON i.object_id = t.object_id
   AND i.name = kc.name
JOIN sys.index_columns ic
    ON ic.object_id = t.object_id
   AND ic.index_id = i.index_id
JOIN sys.columns c
    ON c.object_id = t.object_id
   AND c.column_id = ic.column_id
order by TableName
** */

===== VIEW dbo.rpt_file_custom_view =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[rpt_file_custom_view]
AS
	SELECT customreport_id=cust.id_rpt_file, customrdl_name=cust.rdl_name, customfriendly_name=cust.friendly_name, cust.systemreport_id
	, systemrdl_name=syst.rdl_name, systemfriendly_name=syst.friendly_name
	FROM rpt_file cust WITH(NOLOCK) 
	LEFT JOIN rpt_file syst WITH(NOLOCK) ON syst.iscustom=0 AND syst.id_rpt_file=cust.systemreport_id 
	WHERE cust.iscustom=1

===== VIEW dbo.rs_snmpDevices =====
CREATE   view dbo.rs_snmpDevices
as
	SELECT 
	  dd.deviceid, dd.fclass, dd.id_doma, dd.colorhex
	, dd.name, dd.rack, dd.srow, dd.erow, dd.pingable, dd.ipaddress
	, dve.errors
	FROM (
		SELECT id_device=ISNULL(dv.parentid, dv.deviceid), errors=SUM(snmperr.errors)
		FROM dbo.rs_viewDevices dv
		OUTER APPLY (
		  SELECT errors=COUNT(ipaddress) 
		  FROM snmperror_syn WITH(NOLOCK) 
		  WHERE ipaddress is not null and ipaddress=dv.ipaddress and state=1 and severity>=2
		) snmperr
		GROUP BY ISNULL(dv.parentid, dv.deviceid)
	) dve
	JOIN dbo.rs_viewDevices dd ON dd.deviceid=dve.id_device

===== VIEW dbo.rs_snmpRacks =====
CREATE   view dbo.rs_snmpRacks
as
	SELECT r.id_rackdef, r.rackname, r.nrunits, r.room, dev.devices, dev.errors 
	FROM rs_rackdef r WITH(NOLOCK) 
	OUTER APPLY (
		SELECT 
		  devices=COUNT(DISTINCT deviceid)
		  , errors=SUM(errors) 
		  FROM dbo.rs_snmpDevices 
		  WHERE rack=r.rackname 
	) dev

===== VIEW dbo.rs_viewConnSchemaParent =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[rs_viewConnSchemaParent]
AS
SELECT     dbo.rs_designConn.ID_DESIGNCONN, dbo.rs_designConn.DEVICEIDFROM, dbo.rs_designConn.DEVICEIDTO, rs_devices_1.parentId AS parentId1, 
                      dbo.rs_devices.parentId AS parentId2, dbo.rs_designConn.SCHEMATICSID
FROM         dbo.rs_designConn INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices ON dbo.rs_designConn.DEVICEIDTO = dbo.rs_devices.deviceId INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices AS rs_devices_1 ON dbo.rs_designConn.DEVICEIDFROM = rs_devices_1.deviceId

===== VIEW dbo.rs_viewDevices =====
CREATE   view dbo.rs_viewDevices
as
	SELECT 
	  d.deviceid, d.parentid, d.fclass, d.id_doma
	, dprop.colorhex
	, dxmlfdata.name, dxmlfdata.rack, dxmlfdata.srow, dxmlfdata.erow, dxmlfdata.ipaddress, dxmlfdata.ipraw, dxmlfdata.pingable, dxmlfdata.dal
	, dxmlfdata.cleanuppollfreq, dxmlfdata.cleanupused, dxmlfdata.cleanupwfid, dxmlfdata.cleanupmaxwfstart, cleanupsavedqueryid--, cleanupsavedquery
	FROM rs_devices d WITH(NOLOCK) 
	LEFT JOIN rs_devicesprop dprop WITH(NOLOCK) ON dprop.deviceid=d.deviceid
	OUTER APPLY (SELECT fdata = CAST(d.fdata as xml)) dxml
	OUTER APPLY (
	  SELECT 
	    name = n.c.value('(/param/@name)[1]', 'nvarchar(500)')
	  , rack = ISNULL(n.c.value('(/param/@rack)[1]', 'nvarchar(500)'), '')
	  , srow = n.c.value('(/param/@srow)[1]', 'int')
	  , erow = n.c.value('(/param/@erow)[1]', 'int')
	  , ipaddress = dbo.NormalizeIp(n.c.value('(/param/@ip)[1]', 'nvarchar(50)'))
	  , ipraw = n.c.value('(/param/@ip)[1]', 'nvarchar(50)')
	  , pingable = n.c.value('(/param/@pingable)[1]', 'bit')
	  , dal = n.c.value('(/param/@dal)[1]', 'nvarchar(500)') 
	  , cleanuppollfreq = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanuppollfreq)[1]', 'int')
	  , cleanupused = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanupused)[1]', 'int')
	  , cleanupwfid = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanupwfid)[1]', 'int')
	  , cleanupmaxwfstart = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanupmaxwfstart)[1]', 'int')
	  , cleanupsavedqueryid = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanupsavedqueryid)[1]', 'int')
	  --, cleanupsavedquery = n.c.value('(/param/@cleanupsavedquery)[1]', 'nvarchar(max)')
	  FROM dxml.fdata.nodes('/') n(c)
	) dxmlfdata

===== VIEW dbo.rs_viewRolesConnection =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[rs_viewRolesConnection]
AS
SELECT     dbo.rs_roles.ID_ROLES, dbo.rs_roles.COD_USER, dbo.rs_roles.ID_MODULES, dbo.rs_modules.DESCRIPTION, dbo.rs_schematics.schematicId, 
                      dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId1, dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId2, rs_devices_1.name AS deviceId1Name, dbo.rs_devices.name AS deviceId2Name, 
                      dbo.rs_lock.ID_LOCK, dbo.rs_lock.LOCKTYPE, dbo.rs_lock.DATE, dbo.rs_lock.PROCESSID, dbo.rs_lock.COMPUTER, dbo.rs_lock.APPLICATION
FROM         dbo.rs_roles INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_schematics ON dbo.rs_roles.SCHEMATICSID = dbo.rs_schematics.schematicId INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_modules ON dbo.rs_roles.ID_MODULES = dbo.rs_modules.ID_MODULES INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices AS rs_devices_1 ON dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId1 = rs_devices_1.deviceId INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices ON dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId2 = dbo.rs_devices.deviceId LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_lock ON dbo.rs_schematics.schematicId = dbo.rs_lock.SCHEMATICSID

===== VIEW dbo.rs_viewSchemaParent =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[rs_viewSchemaParent]
AS
SELECT     dbo.rs_schematics.schematicId, dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId1, dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId2, rs_devices_1.parentId AS parentId1, 
                      dbo.rs_devices.parentId AS parentId2,dbo.rs_schematics.tclass,dbo.rs_schematics.visible
FROM         dbo.rs_schematics INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices AS rs_devices_1 ON dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId1 = rs_devices_1.deviceId INNER JOIN
                      dbo.rs_devices ON dbo.rs_schematics.deviceId2 = dbo.rs_devices.deviceId

===== VIEW dbo.si_viewcounter =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.si_viewcounter
AS 
	SELECT c.*, a.*
	FROM si_counter c WITH(NOLOCK) 
	LEFT JOIN si_counteralarm  ca WITH(NOLOCK) ON c.id_counter=ca.id_counter 
	LEFT JOIN si_alarm a WITH(NOLOCK) ON a.id_alarm=ca.id_alarm

===== VIEW dbo.si_viewdata =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.si_viewdata
AS 
	SELECT d.*, counter=c.description, pc=r.name, r.ipaddress
	FROM si_data d WITH(NOLOCK) 
	JOIN si_counter c WITH(NOLOCK) ON c.id_counter=d.id_counter
	JOIN dbo.rs_viewDevices r WITH(NOLOCK) ON r.deviceid=d.deviceid

===== VIEW dbo.SolarTPalinse =====
CREATE   View dbo.SolarTPalinse as
Select  *, 
dbo._GetRightDateByFrame(Data, Ora, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) Solar_Date , 
dbo._GetRightDateByFrame(Data_P, Ora_P, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) Solar_Date_P , 
dbo._fn_hmsf(dbo._GetRightHourByFrame(Ora, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)), dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) Solar_Hour ,
dbo._fn_hmsf(dbo._GetRightHourByFrame(Ora_p, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)), dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) Solar_Hour_p , 
dbo._fn_hmsf(TimeCode_I, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) EventMarkIn, 
dbo._fn_hmsf(TimeCode_O, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) EventMarkOut, 
dbo._fn_hmsf(Duration, dbo.getVideoStandard(cod_user)) EventDuration
from TPalinse with (nolock)
where (cod_user>0)

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.TPalinse_DelEventHistory =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[TPalinse_DelEventHistory] ON [dbo].[TPALINSE]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  delete eventhistory with (rowlock)
  where ID_TPalinse in (select ID_TPalinse from deleted)

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.TPalinse_DelSecEvents =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[TPalinse_DelSecEvents] ON [dbo].[TPALINSE]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  begin tran
    declare @id int
    declare SecEvents cursor for select id_tpalinse from deleted 
    open SecEvents
    fetch next from SecEvents into @id
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      delete from tsec where id_event=@id
      fetch next from SecEvents into @id   
    end 
    close SecEvents
    deallocate SecEvents
  commit tran

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.TPalinse_DelVirtualDocument =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[TPalinse_DelVirtualDocument] ON [dbo].[TPALINSE]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
AS
  begin tran
    declare @id int
    declare documents cursor for select ID_DOCUMENT from deleted
    open documents
    fetch next from documents into @id
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@id > 0) exec dbo.Delete_Documento_Virtuale  @id
      fetch next from documents into @id
    end
    close documents
    deallocate documents
  commit tran

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.tpalinse_lastupdate =====
create trigger tpalinse_lastupdate
on tpalinse
for update
not for replication
as
begin
	set nocount on
	if not update(lastupdate) and
		not update(lastupdatetime) and
		not update(type) 
	begin
		if not update(ora)
		begin
			update t
			set 
				lastupdate = getdate()
			from tpalinse t 
			join inserted on inserted.id_tpalinse = t.id_tpalinse
			update t
			set 
				lastupdatetime = getdate()
			from tpalinse t 
			join inserted on inserted.id_tpalinse = t.id_tpalinse and t.lastupdatetime is null
		end else
		begin
			update t
			set 
				lastupdatetime = getdate()
			from tpalinse t 
			join inserted on inserted.id_tpalinse = t.id_tpalinse		
			
			update t
			set 
				lastupdate = getdate()
			from tpalinse t 
			join inserted on inserted.id_tpalinse = t.id_tpalinse and t.lastupdate is null			
		end	
	end
end

===== VIEW dbo.TPalinseRaggruppaInCluster =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.TPalinseRaggruppaInCluster as
SELECT     t.DATA, t.COD_USER, t.LIVELLO, t.DATA_P, t.ORA_P, MIN(t.ORA) AS Ora_Inizio_Break, MIN(t.ORA) + SUM(t.DURATION) AS Ora_Fine_Break, 
                      'BREAK ' + dbo._fn_hms(t.ORA_P, dbo.getVideoStandard(t.COD_USER)) AS Codice_Break, '___B' AS newtype, COUNT(t.ID_TPALINSE) 
                      AS Totale_Eventi, MIN(t.XORDER) AS xorder_First, MAX(t.XORDER) AS xorder_Last
FROM         dbo.tpalinse AS t WITH (nolock) INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tipologieprop AS p WITH (nolock) ON p.COD_TYPE = t.NEWTYPE
WHERE     (p.PROP = 'oiRaggruppaInCluster')
GROUP BY t.DATA, t.COD_USER, t.LIVELLO, t.DATA_P, t.ORA_P

===== VIEW dbo.TPalinseSpotsInCluster =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.TPalinseSpotsInCluster as
SELECT     tr.xorder_First, tr.xorder_Last, tr.Ora_Inizio_Break, tr.Ora_Fine_Break, tr.Codice_Break, 
           t.*
FROM         dbo.tpalinse AS t with (nolock) INNER JOIN
                      dbo.TPalinseRaggruppaInCluster AS tr with (nolock) ON t.DATA = tr.data AND t.COD_USER = tr.cod_user AND t.LIVELLO = tr.livello AND t.DATA_P = tr.data_p AND 
                      t.ORA_P = tr.ora_p AND t.XORDER >= tr.xorder_First AND t.XORDER <= tr.xorder_Last

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_DayStructure =====
CREATE   View dbo.Traffic_DayStructure as
Select  TC.Date, TC.Cod_User,
TSch.Name ScheduleName, TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule,
TB.Name BlockName,TS.ID_TrafficBlock,ts.ObjectNumber,ts.Split,ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, ts.Groups,ts.BudgetActive,ts.BudgetPassive,ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,ts.ID_TrafficSegment,ts.Type,ts.RowGuid,ts.offset,ts.duration,ts.maxduration,
TSB.Offset BlockHour, (TSB.Offset + TS.Offset) SegmentHour, 0 PalinseSplit, TC.[Level]
from Traffic_Schedule TSch with (nolock)
join Traffic_ScheduleBlock TSB with (nolock) on TSB.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
join Traffic_Block TB with (nolock) on TB.ID_TrafficBlock = TSB.ID_TrafficBlock
join (
select DISTINCT
		TS.ID_TrafficBlock,
		ts.ObjectNumber, 
		ts.Split, 
		ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, 
		ts.Groups,
		ts.BudgetActive, 
		ts.BudgetPassive, 
		ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,
		ISNULL(t1.ID_TrafficSegment,t2.ID_TrafficSegment) as ID_TrafficSegment,
		ISNULL(t1.Type, t2.Type)as Type,
		ISNULL(t1.RowGuid, t2.RowGuid) as RowGuid,
		ISNULL(T1.Offset, t2.Offset) offset,
		ISNULL(T1.Duration, t2.Duration) duration,
		ISNULL(T1.MaxDuration, t2.MaxDuration) maxduration
	from Traffic_Segment ts with(nolock)
	LEFT join Trf_instanceSegment t2 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t2.ID_TrafficBlock
	LEFT join Traffic_Segment t1 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t1.ID_TrafficBlock AND t2.ID_INSTANCESEGMENT IS NULL  
) TS on TS.ID_TrafficBlock=TB.ID_TrafficBlock
join Traffic_Calendar TC with (nolock) on TC.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
where TS.Split = 0 or TS.split=1

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_DayStructureEx =====
CREATE   View dbo.Traffic_DayStructureEx as
Select DS.*, Dbo.GetRightDuration(SS.TotalDuration) TotalDuration, SS.Max_Priority, SS.Min_Priority, SS.ObjNum ObjPresent,
	dbo._fn_hmsf(DS.SegmentHour, (select dbo.EnvStr('videostandard',DS.Cod_User ))) SegmentHourHMSF, dbo._fn_hmsf(SS.TotalDuration, (select dbo.EnvStr('videostandard',DS.Cod_User ))) TotalDurationHMSF,
	(DS.Duration - Dbo.GetRightDuration(SS.TotalDuration)) FreeSpace
from Traffic_DayStructure DS with(nolock)
left join Traffic_SegmentSummary SS with(nolock) on (SS.ID_TrafficBlock = DS.ID_TrafficBlock and SS.ID_TrafficSegment = DS.ID_TrafficSegment
	and SS.Data = DS.Date and SS.Cod_User = DS.Cod_User and SS.Split = dbo.NullToZero(DS.PalinseSplit))

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_DayStructureEx_Calc =====
CREATE   view dbo.Traffic_DayStructureEx_Calc as
select [Date], ID_TrafficSchedule, BlockName, ID_TrafficSegment, ID_TrafficBlock, Offset, Duration,
	ObjectNumber, Type, PalinseSplit, MaxDuration, BlockHour, SegmentHour, Sum(TotalDuration) TotalDuration,
	Max(Max_Priority) Max_Priority, Min(Min_Priority) Min_Priority, Sum(ObjPresent) ObjPresent, Cod_User
from Traffic_DayStructureEx with(nolock)
group by [Date], ID_TrafficSchedule, BlockName, ID_TrafficSegment, ID_TrafficBlock, Offset, Duration, ObjectNumber,
	 Type, PalinseSplit, MaxDuration, BlockHour, SegmentHour, Cod_User

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_DayStructureWithOutSplit =====
CREATE   View dbo.Traffic_DayStructureWithOutSplit as
Select  TC.Date, TC.Cod_User,
TSch.Name ScheduleName, TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule,
TB.Name BlockName,TS.ID_TrafficBlock,ts.ObjectNumber,ts.Split,ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, ts.Groups,ts.BudgetActive,ts.BudgetPassive,ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,ts.ID_TrafficSegment,ts.Type,ts.RowGuid,ts.offset,ts.duration,ts.maxduration,
TSB.Offset BlockHour, (TSB.Offset + TS.Offset) SegmentHour, 0 PalinseSplit, TC.[Level]
from Traffic_Schedule TSch with (nolock)
join Traffic_ScheduleBlock TSB with (nolock) on TSB.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
join Traffic_Block TB with (nolock) on TB.ID_TrafficBlock = TSB.ID_TrafficBlock
join (
select DISTINCT
		TS.ID_TrafficBlock,
		ts.ObjectNumber, 
		ts.Split, 
		ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, 
		ts.Groups,
		ts.BudgetActive, 
		ts.BudgetPassive, 
		ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,
		ISNULL(t1.ID_TrafficSegment,t2.ID_TrafficSegment) as ID_TrafficSegment,
		ISNULL(t1.Type, t2.Type)as Type,
		ISNULL(t1.RowGuid, t2.RowGuid) as RowGuid,
		ISNULL(T1.Offset, t2.Offset) offset,
		ISNULL(T1.Duration, t2.Duration) duration,
		ISNULL(T1.MaxDuration, t2.MaxDuration) maxduration
	from Traffic_Segment ts with(nolock)
	LEFT join Trf_instanceSegment t2 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t2.ID_TrafficBlock
	LEFT join Traffic_Segment t1 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t1.ID_TrafficBlock AND t2.ID_INSTANCESEGMENT IS NULL  
) TS on TS.ID_TrafficBlock=TB.ID_TrafficBlock
join Traffic_Calendar TC with (nolock) on TC.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
where TS.Split = 0

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_DayStructureWithSplit =====
CREATE   View dbo.Traffic_DayStructureWithSplit as
Select  TC.Date, TC.Cod_User,
TSch.Name ScheduleName, TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule,
TB.Name BlockName,TS.ID_TrafficBlock,ts.ObjectNumber,ts.Split,ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, ts.Groups,ts.BudgetActive,ts.BudgetPassive,ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,ts.ID_TrafficSegment,ts.Type,ts.RowGuid,ts.offset,ts.duration,ts.maxduration,
TSB.Offset BlockHour, (TSB.Offset + TS.Offset) SegmentHour, 0 PalinseSplit, TC.[Level]
from Traffic_Schedule TSch with (nolock)
join Traffic_ScheduleBlock TSB with (nolock) on TSB.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
join Traffic_Block TB with (nolock) on TB.ID_TrafficBlock = TSB.ID_TrafficBlock
join (
select DISTINCT
		TS.ID_TrafficBlock,
		ts.ObjectNumber, 
		ts.Split, 
		ts.Notes, 
		ts.ViewOrder, 
		ts.Groups,
		ts.BudgetActive, 
		ts.BudgetPassive, 
		ts.ID_TrafficMusicTemplates, 
		ts.TargetAudience,
		ISNULL(t1.ID_TrafficSegment,t2.ID_TrafficSegment) as ID_TrafficSegment,
		ISNULL(t1.Type, t2.Type)as Type,
		ISNULL(t1.RowGuid, t2.RowGuid) as RowGuid,
		ISNULL(T1.Offset, t2.Offset) offset,
		ISNULL(T1.Duration, t2.Duration) duration,
		ISNULL(T1.MaxDuration, t2.MaxDuration) maxduration
	from Traffic_Segment ts with(nolock)
	LEFT join Trf_instanceSegment t2 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t2.ID_TrafficBlock
	LEFT join Traffic_Segment t1 with(nolock) on ts.ID_TrafficBlock = t1.ID_TrafficBlock AND t2.ID_INSTANCESEGMENT IS NULL  
) TS on TS.ID_TrafficBlock=TB.ID_TrafficBlock
join Traffic_Calendar TC with (nolock) on TC.ID_TrafficSchedule = TSch.ID_TrafficSchedule
where TS.Split = 1

===== VIEW dbo.Traffic_SegmentSummary =====
CREATE   View [dbo].[Traffic_SegmentSummary] as
Select      sum(t.Duration) TotalDuration,max(cr.priorita) Max_Priority,Min(cr.Priorita) Min_Priority,  Count(*) ObjNum,
t.Data, t.Cod_User, tp.id_fascia id_trafficblock, tp.clusterIndex id_trafficsegment, t.Split
from trafficpalinse tp with(nolock)
join tpalinse t with(nolock) on t.ID_TPALINSE=tp.id_tpalinse
left join CONTRATTIRIGHE cr with (nolock) on cr.id_contrattirighe=tp.ID_ContrattiRighe
where (t.Livello = 0 or 
(t.Livello <> 0 and DateDiff(d, GetDate(), tp.scadenza) >= 0))
and  t.duration>cast(dbo.trf_getIniFilesValue('Traffic.ini/%EventDurationNoCalc') as int)
group by t.Data, t.Cod_User, tp.id_fascia,tp.clusterIndex,t.Split

===== VIEW dbo.TrafficForDay =====
CREATE   View dbo.TrafficForDay as
Select Cod_User, Data, Sum(Totale) Totale, Split from _TrafficForDay
group by Data, Cod_User, Split

===== VIEW dbo.TrafficForHour =====
CREATE   view dbo.TrafficForHour as
	Select P.Cod_User,
	dbo.GetRightDate(P.Data, O.Ora,0) Data,
	Dbo.GetRightHour(O.Ora, 0) Ora,
	sum( Dbo.MyMin(O.Fine, (P.Ora + P.Duration)) -
	Dbo.MyMax(O.Inizio, P.Ora) ) Totale, P.Split, 
        dbo._fn_HMSF(sum( Dbo.MyMin(O.Fine, (P.Ora + P.Duration)) -
	Dbo.MyMax(O.Inizio, P.Ora) ),(select dbo.EnvStr('videostandard',P.Cod_User ))) TotaleHMSF
from TPalinse P with (nolock)
join Traffic_Hour O on (O.Cod_User = P.Cod_User and(
	(P.Ora >= O.Inizio and P.Ora <= O.Fine) or
	((P.Ora + P.Duration) >= O.Inizio and (P.Ora + P.Duration) <= O.Fine)))
join Tipologie T on T.Cod_Type = P.NewType
where
	P.Livello = 0 
	and T.Affollamento = 'S'
group by P.Data, P.Cod_User, O.Inizio, O.Ora, P.Split

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.TrafficIDCreate =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[TrafficIDCreate] ON [dbo].[tpalinse]
FOR INSERT
AS
  --if exists(select trafficid from inserted where trafficid<0)
  begin
    update P set P.TrafficID = P.ID_TPalinse
    from TPalinse P with (rowlock)
    join  inserted I on I.id_Tpalinse = P.ID_TPalinse
    where p.TrafficID<=0
  end

===== VIEW dbo.TrafficLight_Contract =====
CREATE   view dbo.TrafficLight_Contract as
  Select  CT.ID_ContrattiTestata, CT.Cod_Contratto ContractCode, CT.Descrizione ContractDescription,
	CT.Data_Acquisizione ContractDate, CT.Data_Inizio ContractStartDate, CT.Data_Termine ContractEndDate,
	CR.ID_ContrattiRighe, CR.Durata RowDuration, CR.NewType RowNewType, CR.Priorita RowPriority,
	CR.DateStart RowStartDate, CR.DateEnd RowEndDate,
	CR.N_Passaggi RowTotPass, CR.Descrizione RowDescription, CR.Cod_User RowCod_User, CR.Nielsen RowNielsen,
	CR.Passaggi_Giornalieri RowDailyPass, CR.Intervallo RowSameRowInterval, CR.Ora_InizioF RowStartTimeF, CR.Ora_FineF RowEndTimeF,  --CR.Ora_Inizio RowStartTime, CR.Ora_Fine RowEndTime, 
	CR.Interv_Committente RowCustomerInterval, CR.Interv_Contratto RowContractInterval,
	CR.Lunedi RowMon, CR.Martedi RowTue, CR.Mercoledi RowWed, CR.Giovedi RowThu, CR.Venerdi RowFri, CR.Sabato RowSat,
	CR.Domenica RowSun, CR.ControllaCapofila RowStartCheck, CR.ControllaFineFila RowEndCheck,
	CR.ControllaNielsen RowNielsenCheck, 
	--dbo.GetTotaleProgrammatiAsset(CF.ID_Filmati) RowScheduledPassage,
	dbo.NrEventSched(CR.ID_ContrattiRighe, CR.Cod_User) RowScheduledPassage,
	CR.Omaggio RowOmaggio, CR.Ignora_Regole RowIgnoraRegole,
	CF.ID_Filmati, CT.Committente ID_Customer, CT.Ut_Finale ID_FinalUser, CT.CentroMedia ID_MediaCenter, 
	CT.Agenzia ID_Agency
  from ContrattiTestata CT with (nolock)
  join ContrattiRighe CR with (nolock) on CT.ID_ContrattiTestata = CR.ID_ContrattiTestata
  join ContrattiFilmati CF with (nolock) on CF.ID_ContrattiRighe = CR.ID_ContrattiRighe
  where CF.ID_Filmati > 0 and CT.Flag = 0 and CT.contracttype=0

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.trafficpalinse_delMultiContractRow =====
CREATE   trigger trafficpalinse_delMultiContractRow
on trafficpalinse
FOR DELETE --not for replication
as
begin
  delete trf_trafficpalinseMultiContract with(rowlock) where id_trafficpalinse in (select id_trafficPalinse from deleted)	
end
