CREATE   trigger [dbo].[trafficpalinse_delrights]
on [dbo].[trafficPalinse]
FOR DELETE --not for replication
as
begin
  delete rig_rights with (rowlock)  where ID_TPalinse in (select ID_TPalinse from deleted)	
  delete Rig_rights with (rowlock)  where ID_TPalinseexclude in (select ID_TPalinse from deleted)	
end

===== VIEW dbo.trafficTPalinse =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[trafficTPalinse]
AS
	SELECT P.id_trafficPalinse, P.id_palinsesto ID_TrafficSchedule, P.id_fascia ID_TrafficBlock,
	P.clusterIndex ID_TrafficSegment, P.Offset, P.ID_ContrattiRighe, P.ID_Operation, P.scadenza,
	CR.PRIORITA, CR.NIELSEN, P.ID_FatturaAgenzia, P.ID_FatturaEmittente,P.failcalculate,
	TP.ID_TPalinse, TP.Cod_Progra, TP.Title, TP.Livello, TP.Split, TP.Ordinale, TP.ID_Filmati,
	TP.Cod_User, TP.Data, TP.Ora, TP.Data_P, TP.Ora_P, TP.Duration, Tp.Supporto,
	TP.Status, TP.NewType, TP.Part, TP.TimeCode_I, TP.TimeCode_O, TP.Event_P, TP.Event_Type, P.[Date] TrafficDate, 
	TP.ID_Document, TP.TRAFFICID, P.TrafficFlag, P.TrafficNotes, P.ID_FatturaEmittenteLOGO,
	TP.Titler_In, TP.Dsk1, TP.Titler_Dur, TP.Dsk2,TP.xorder, CR.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA, P.EVENTAMMOUNT,TP.TRF_EVENTLEVEL,TP.ASPECT,TP.code_primecast,isnull(PC.description,'') primecastdesc,p.eventtype,TP.DURATION_P as DURATION_P,
	isnull(TP.crawl_Desc,'') crawl_Desc,tp.schedule_checksum,P.ID_CPEMITTENTE,P.ID_CPAGENZIA,P.ID_CPEMITTENTELOGO,id_split_start
	FROM trafficPalinse P WITH (NOLOCK)
	INNER JOIN TPALINSE TP WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.id_tpalinse = TP.id_tpalinse
	LEFT OUTER JOIN CONTRATTIRIGHE CR WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE = CR.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE
 	LEFT OUTER JOIN contrattitestata AS CT WITH (nolock) ON CR.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA = CT.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA
	LEFT OUTER JOIN PRIMECAST PC WITH (nolock) ON PC.CODE=TP.code_primecast

===== VIEW dbo.trafficTPalinseReport =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[trafficTPalinseReport]
AS
	SELECT P.id_trafficPalinse, P.id_palinsesto ID_TrafficSchedule, P.id_fascia ID_TrafficBlock,
	P.clusterIndex ID_TrafficSegment, P.Offset, isnull(tc.id_contrattirighechild,P.id_contrattirighe) ID_ContrattiRighe, P.ID_Operation, P.scadenza,
	CR.PRIORITA, CR.NIELSEN, P.ID_FatturaAgenzia, P.ID_FatturaEmittente,P.failcalculate,
	TP.ID_TPalinse, TP.Cod_Progra, TP.Title, TP.Livello, TP.Split, TP.Ordinale, TP.ID_Filmati,
	TP.Cod_User, TP.Data, TP.Ora, TP.Data_P, TP.Ora_P, TP.Duration, Tp.Supporto,
	TP.Status, TP.NewType, TP.Part, TP.TimeCode_I, TP.TimeCode_O, TP.Event_P, TP.Event_Type, P.[Date] TrafficDate, 
	TP.ID_Document, TP.TRAFFICID, P.TrafficFlag, P.TrafficNotes, P.ID_FatturaEmittenteLOGO,
	TP.Titler_In, TP.Dsk1, TP.Titler_Dur, TP.Dsk2,TP.xorder,tc.id_contrattitestatachild as id_contrattitestata, P.EVENTAMMOUNT,TP.TRF_EVENTLEVEL,TP.ASPECT,TP.code_primecast,isnull(PC.description,'') primecastdesc,p.eventtype,TP.DURATION_P as DURATION_P,
	isnull(TP.crawl_Desc,'') crawl_Desc,tp.schedule_checksum
	FROM trafficPalinse P WITH (NOLOCK)
	INNER JOIN TPALINSE TP WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.id_tpalinse = TP.id_tpalinse
	join trf_contrattirigheMultiContract tc on tc.id_contrattirigheMaster=p.ID_ContrattiRighe
	LEFT OUTER JOIN CONTRATTIRIGHE CR WITH (NOLOCK) ON CR.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE = tc.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHEchild
 	LEFT OUTER JOIN contrattitestata AS CT WITH (nolock) ON CR.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA = CT.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA
	LEFT OUTER JOIN PRIMECAST PC WITH (nolock) ON PC.CODE=TP.code_primecast
	UNION
	SELECT P.id_trafficPalinse, P.id_palinsesto ID_TrafficSchedule, P.id_fascia ID_TrafficBlock,
	P.clusterIndex ID_TrafficSegment, P.Offset, P.ID_ContrattiRighe, P.ID_Operation, P.scadenza,
	CR.PRIORITA, CR.NIELSEN, P.ID_FatturaAgenzia, P.ID_FatturaEmittente,P.failcalculate,
	TP.ID_TPalinse, TP.Cod_Progra, TP.Title, TP.Livello, TP.Split, TP.Ordinale, TP.ID_Filmati,
	TP.Cod_User, TP.Data, TP.Ora, TP.Data_P, TP.Ora_P, TP.Duration, Tp.Supporto,
	TP.Status, TP.NewType, TP.Part, TP.TimeCode_I, TP.TimeCode_O, TP.Event_P, TP.Event_Type, P.[Date] TrafficDate, 
	TP.ID_Document, TP.TRAFFICID, P.TrafficFlag, P.TrafficNotes, P.ID_FatturaEmittenteLOGO,
	TP.Titler_In, TP.Dsk1, TP.Titler_Dur, TP.Dsk2,TP.xorder, CR.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA, P.EVENTAMMOUNT,TP.TRF_EVENTLEVEL,TP.ASPECT,TP.code_primecast,isnull(PC.description,'') primecastdesc,p.eventtype,TP.DURATION_P as DURATION_P,
	isnull(TP.crawl_Desc,'') crawl_Desc,tp.schedule_checksum
	FROM trafficPalinse P WITH (NOLOCK)
	INNER JOIN TPALINSE TP WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.id_tpalinse = TP.id_tpalinse
	LEFT OUTER JOIN CONTRATTIRIGHE CR WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE = CR.ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE
 	LEFT OUTER JOIN contrattitestata AS CT WITH (nolock) ON CR.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA = CT.ID_CONTRATTITESTATA
	LEFT OUTER JOIN PRIMECAST PC WITH (nolock) ON PC.CODE=TP.code_primecast
	WHERE CR.MULTICONTRACT IS NULL

===== SQL_SCALAR_FUNCTION dbo.trf_contractTimeToFrame =====
CREATE   FUNCTION [dbo].[trf_contractTimeToFrame](@ora int,@oraf int,@coduser int,@type nvarchar(1))
returns int
/*$ifdef >=sql2019*//* */
/*WITH INLINE = OFF, ENCRYPTION*/
/**//*$endif*/
as
begin
	--type = 'E' end time - 'S' start time
	declare @r int
	set @r=@oraf
	if (isnull(@oraf,-1)<0)
	begin
		if (@ora<=24)
		begin
			if (upper(@type)='E')
				set @r=dbo._SecToFrames(@ora*3600,dbo.getVideoStandard(@coduser))+dbo.tcGetFramesPerDay(dbo.getVideoStandard(@coduser))
			else
				if (@ora<>0)
					set @r=dbo._SecToFrames(@ora*3600,dbo.getVideoStandard(@coduser))
				else
					set @r=0
		end	
	end
  return @r
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.TRG_FILMATI_UPDATE =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.[TRG_FILMATI_UPDATE] ON [dbo].[filmati]
FOR UPDATE
AS
begin
declare @description nvarchar(200)
declare @ID_Serie int
declare @Count int
if update (Descrizio)
begin
	Select @description = Descrizio, @ID_Serie = ID_Serie from inserted
	Select @Count = count(*) from Filmati with (nolock) where id_serie = @ID_Serie
	if @Count = 1 
		Update FSerie set Descrizio = @Description where id_Serie = @ID_Serie
end
end

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.trig_del_storico =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.trig_del_storico ON [dbo].[tpalinse_locktable]
FOR DELETE
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT INTO tpalinse_storicolock  with (rowlock) (paldate, refcount, iduser, owner, state, livello, groupid)
	SELECT DEL.paldate, DEL.refcount, DEL.iduser, DEL.owner, 0, DEL.livello, DEL.groupid
	FROM deleted DEL with (nolock)
END

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.trig_ins_storico =====
CREATE   TRIGGER dbo.trig_ins_storico ON [dbo].[tpalinse_locktable]
FOR INSERT
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT INTO tpalinse_storicolock with (rowlock) (paldate, refcount, iduser, owner, state, livello, groupid)
	SELECT INS.paldate, INS.refcount, INS.iduser, INS.owner, 1, INS.livello, INS.groupid 
	FROM inserted INS with (nolock)
END

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.tsec_lastupdate =====
CREATE   trigger tsec_lastupdate
on tsec
for insert,update,delete
--not for replication
as
begin
  set nocount on
  --if not update(lastupdate) and
  --not update(type)
  begin
    update t
    set 
        lastupdate = getdate()
    from tpalinse t 
    join inserted on inserted.id_event = t.id_tpalinse
    update t
    set 
        lastupdate = getdate()
    from tpalinse t 
    join deleted on deleted.id_event = t.id_tpalinse
  end
end

===== VIEW dbo.unique_keys =====
CREATE   view dbo.unique_keys as
  select distinct 
    tbl.name TableName, 
    constrId.name PkName, 
    col.name ColName, 
    sik.keyno,
    case when ix.indid = 1 then 1 else 0 end IsClustered
  from sysobjects tbl 
    join sysconstraints constr on ( tbl.id = constr.id and tbl.xtype = 'U' and constr.status & 0x0001 = 0x0001 )
    join sysobjects constrId on constrId.parent_obj = tbl.id and constrId.xtype in ('UQ')
    join sysindexes ix on constrId.name = ix.name and ix.id = tbl.id
    join sysindexkeys sik on sik.id = tbl.id and sik.indid = ix.indid
    join syscolumns col on col.id = tbl.id and sik.colid = col.colid
/* babelfish version also valid for MS SQL **
SELECT DISTINCT
    t.name AS TableName,
    kc.name AS PkName,
    c.name AS ColName,
    ic.key_ordinal AS keyno,
    CASE WHEN i.type = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsClustered
FROM sys.tables t
JOIN sys.key_constraints kc
    ON kc.parent_object_id = t.object_id
   AND kc.type IN ('UQ')
JOIN sys.indexes i
    ON i.object_id = t.object_id
   AND i.name = kc.name
JOIN sys.index_columns ic
    ON ic.object_id = t.object_id
   AND ic.index_id = i.index_id
JOIN sys.columns c
    ON c.object_id = t.object_id
   AND c.column_id = ic.column_id
order by TableName
** */

===== VIEW dbo.VIEW_Scadenze =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VIEW_Scadenze AS
	Select F.*, S.Importo, S.Scadenza, S.ID_Scadenze from EnvoiceList F
	join Scadenze S on S.ID_FatturaTestata = F.ID_FatturaTestata

===== VIEW dbo.VwAllFSupporti =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VwAllFSupporti
AS
SELECT ST.supportType,TT.Desc_tapetypes AS Tipo_cassetta, Stato = (CASE PM.flags 
							WHEN 'f' THEN '1'
							WHEN 'i' THEN '2'
							WHEN 'o' THEN '3'
							 ELSE '0' END),
	id_fprestiti,id_fprestmulti,description,eticons, S.*
FROM FSupporti S with (nolock)
LEFT JOIN TapeTypes TT with (nolock) ON S.Cod_tapetypes = TT.ID_Tapetypes
LEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT Id_Supporti,Flags, id_fprestiti,id_fprestmulti 
	      FROM FPrestitiMulti with (nolock)
	      WHERE Flags='f' OR Flags='o' OR Flags='i'
	     ) PM ON S.Id_Supporti = PM.Id_Supporti
LEFT JOIN FSupp_Types ST with (nolock) ON substring(S.supporto,6,5)=ST.supp_type

===== VIEW dbo.VWAllTapes =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VWAllTapes]
AS
SELECT S.*,T.description TapeTypeDesc,T.eticons
FROM FSupporti S with (nolock) 
LEFT JOIN FSupp_Types T with (nolock) ON substring(S.supporto,6,5)=T.supp_type

===== VIEW dbo.VwAnagReparti =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VwAnagReparti
AS
SELECT Rep.Id_anagrafReparti GroupOrd, Pers.*				
FROM (SELECT Id_anagrafReparti FROM anagrafReparti WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE Id_reparto=0) Rep
LEFT JOIN (SELECT * FROM anagrafReparti WITH (NOLOCK) ) Pers 
ON (Rep.Id_anagrafReparti=Pers.Id_reparto OR 
(Rep.Id_anagrafReparti=Pers.Id_anagrafReparti AND Pers.Id_reparto=0))

===== VIEW dbo.VwContainer =====

	select 'MOV' Container
	union
	select 'MXF' Container
	union
	select 'MPG' Container
	union
	select 'AVI' Container
	union
	select 'GXF' Container
	union
	select 'MP4' Container
	union
	select 'TS' Container

===== VIEW dbo.VwContrattiRighe =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwContrattiRighe]
AS
	select ID_CONTRATTIRIGHE, ID_CONTRATTITESTATA, DURATA, PRIORITA, IMPORTO, N_PUNTATE, N_PASSAGGI, DESCRIZIONE, 
		COD_USER, PASSAGGI_GIORNALIERI, PASSAGGI_SETTIMANALI, ORA_INIZIO, ORA_FINE, SCADENZA, LUNEDI, MARTEDI, 
		MERCOLEDI, GIOVEDI, VENERDI, SABATO, DOMENICA, IGNORA_REGOLE, CONTROLLACAPOFILA, CONTROLLAFINEFILA, 
		DATA_INIZIO, DATA_FINE, N_PASSXPUNTATA, PrioritaWhiteList, DATESTART, DATEEND, EVENTLEVEL, ORA_INIZIOF, ORA_FINEF
		,SCH_IMPORTO = case when controllaMiddle=1 then IMPORTO/3 when controllacapofila=1 and controllafinefila=1 and controllaMiddle=0 then IMPORTO/2 else IMPORTO end 
		,SCH_Divider = case when controllaMiddle=1 then 3 when controllacapofila=1 and controllafinefila=1 and controllaMiddle=0 then 2 else 1 end 
	from contrattirighe with (nolock)

===== VIEW dbo.VwCustomer =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwCustomer]
AS
	Select distinct A.ID_ANAGRAF,A.COD_CONTO,A.RAG_SOCIAL,A.FlagAgent, A.TIPO_DITTA, A.TIPO_CLI, A.AGENTE1, A.AGENTE2, A.AGENTE3, A.AGENTE4, A.AGENTE5 
	FROM Anagraf A with (nolock) 
	join contrattitestata C with (nolock) on A.ID_ANAGRAF= C.COMMITTENTE

===== VIEW dbo.VWDataTapes =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VWDataTapes]
AS
SELECT S.*,T.description TapeTypeDesc,T.eticons
FROM FSupporti S with (nolock) 
LEFT JOIN FSupp_Types T with (nolock) ON substring(S.supporto,6,5)=T.supp_type
WHERE isnull(T.SupportType,0)=2

===== VIEW dbo.VwFSerie =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VwFSerie
AS
Select 
S.ID_Serie, S.Descrizio, S.NewType, S.Data_Prod, S.Data_Arrivo, FS.Num, S.season, Expired = case when getdate() > S.Data_scad then 1 else 0 end   
from FSerie S with (nolock)
left join (Select count(distinct puntata) Num, ID_Serie from Filmati with (nolock) group by ID_Serie) FS on FS.ID_Serie = S.ID_Serie

===== VIEW dbo.VwFSupporti =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VwFSupporti
AS
SELECT ST.supportType,TT.Desc_tapetypes AS Tipo_cassetta, Stato = (CASE PM.flags 
							WHEN 'f' THEN '1'
							WHEN 'i' THEN '2'
							WHEN 'o' THEN '3'
							 ELSE '0' END),
	id_fprestiti,id_fprestmulti,description,eticons, S.*
FROM FSupporti S with (nolock) 
LEFT JOIN TapeTypes TT with (nolock) ON S.Cod_tapetypes = TT.ID_Tapetypes
LEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT Id_Supporti,Flags, id_fprestiti,id_fprestmulti 
	      FROM FPrestitiMulti with (nolock) 
	      WHERE Flags='f' OR Flags='o' OR Flags='i'
	     ) PM ON S.Id_Supporti = PM.Id_Supporti
LEFT JOIN FSupp_Types ST with (nolock) ON substring(S.supporto,6,5)=ST.supp_type
WHERE (ISNULL(S.Deleted,0) <> 1)

===== VIEW dbo.VwFSupportiLive =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.VwFSupportiLive
AS
Select * FROM FSupporti with (nolock) WHERE (ISNULL(Deleted,0) <> 1)

===== VIEW dbo.VwPromo =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwPromo]
AS
select id_filmati,cod_progra,descrizio,newtype,Id_serie,durata, data_inizio_validita, data_scad, data_arrivo, Id_Fornitore, enableddays, frequency   
from filmati F with (nolock)
where newtype in 
(select cod_type from tipologieprop TP with (nolock) where prop in ('oiPromo','oiAffollamentoPromo','oiCrossPromo','oiGenericPromo'))

===== VIEW dbo.VwSalesmen =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwSalesmen]
AS
	select ID_ANAGRAF, A.COD_CONTO, A.RAG_SOCIAL, [Description] = case when ltrim(isnull(A.rag_social,''))='' then A.COD_CONTO else A.RAG_SOCIAL end,
		A.TIPO_DITTA, A.TIPO_CLI
	from anagraf A with (nolock) where FlagAgent = 1

===== VIEW dbo.VwScheduledEvents =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwScheduledEvents]
AS
	
	Select 
		id_contrattirighe,
		cod_user,
		NumEvents = (sum (1) / dbo.Trf_GetEventScheduleDivider(id_contrattirighe)), 
		NumTransmitted = (sum (case when Status in ('D','F','G','M','Q') then 1 else 0 end) / dbo.Trf_GetEventScheduleDivider(id_contrattirighe))
	from trafficTpalinse with(nolock) 
	where Livello in (0, 2001, 2002, 2003, 2004, 2005, 2006, 2007, 2008, 2009, 2010) and part in (0,1,99) and eventtype=0
	group by id_contrattirighe,cod_user
	union
	Select --logo
		ts.id_contrattirighe,
		cr.cod_user,
		NumEvents = count(ts.id_contrattirighe),
		NumTransmitted = sum (case when (ts.ASRUN_STATUS_C='D' or ts.ASRUN_STATUS_C='Q' or ts.ASRUN_STATUS_M='D' or ts.ASRUN_STATUS_M='Q') then 1 else 0 end)
	from trafficTpalinse tp with(nolock) 
	join tsec ts with(nolock) on tp.id_tpalinse=ts.id_event
	join contrattirighe cr with(nolock) on cr.id_contrattirighe=ts.id_contrattirighe and CR.Logo = 1
	where Livello in (0, 2001, 2002, 2003, 2004, 2005, 2006, 2007, 2008, 2009, 2010) and eventtype=0
	group by ts.id_contrattirighe, cr.cod_user

	FROM trafficPalinse P WITH (NOLOCK)
	INNER JOIN TPALINSE TP WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.id_tpalinse = TP.ID_Tpalinse and P.eventtype=0 and TP.Livello in (0, 2001, 2002, 2003, 2004, 2005, 2006, 2007, 2008, 2009, 2010)

===== VIEW dbo.VwWBList =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[VwWBList]
AS
	
	Select 
		ID_ContrattiRighe,
		NumBlackList = sum(case when BlackList = 1 then PassageMiss else 0 end),
		NumWhiteList = sum(case when BlackList = 0 then PassageMiss else 0 end)
	from Traffic_ScheduleList
	group by ID_ContrattiRighe

===== VIEW dbo.wf_asrunLog =====
CREATE   view wf_asrunLog
as
    select 
        wi.id_instance as ID_INSTANCE,
        wic.id_instanceclass as ID_INSTANCECLASS,
        wic.friendly_name as INSTANCECLASS_NAME,
        wl.id_log as ID_LOG,
        wa.id_action as ID_ACTION,
        wac.id_actionclass as ID_ACTIONCLASS,
        wac.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME,
        wac.category1 as ACTIONCLASS_CATEGORY,
        wfo.ucode as FOREIGN_OBJECT_CODE,
        wi.foreign_key AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_KEY,
        wl.worker_loginname AS WORKER_LOGINNAME
        from wf_instance wi with (nolock)
            join wf_foreignobject wfo with (nolock) on wfo.id_foreignobject = wi.id_foreignobject
            join wf_log wl with (nolock) on wl.id_instance = wi.id_instance
            join wf_action wa with (nolock) on wl.id_action = wa.id_action
            join wf_actionclass wac with (nolock) on wac.id_actionclass = wa.id_actionclass
            join wf_instanceclass wic with (nolock) on wic.id_instanceclass = wi.id_instanceclass

    join wf_foreignobject fo with (nolock) on fo.id_foreignobject = i.id_foreignobject and fo.ucode='f'

===== VIEW dbo.wf_assetqualitycheck =====
CREATE   VIEW dbo.wf_assetqualitycheck
as
	select 
	I.id_instance,
	I.foreign_key AS ID_FILMATI,
	IC.id_instanceclass,
	IC.friendly_name as INSTANCECLASS_NAME,
	J.id_job,
	A.id_action,
	AC.id_actionclass,
	AC.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME
	from wf_instance I with (nolock)
	    join wf_foreignobject FO with (nolock) on FO.id_foreignobject = I.id_foreignobject and FO.ucode='f'
	    join wf_job J with (nolock) on J.id_instance = I.id_instance
	    join wf_action A with (nolock) on J.id_action = A.id_action
	    join wf_actionclass AC with (nolock) on AC.id_actionclass = A.id_actionclass and AC.ucode = 'af.1.qltchk.act'
	    join wf_instanceclass IC with (nolock) on IC.id_instanceclass = I.id_instanceclass

===== VIEW dbo.wf_assetWebRequests =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[wf_assetWebRequests]
as
	select 
	I.id_instance,
	I.foreign_key AS ID_ANAGRAF,
	I.foreign_key2 AS ID_FILMATI,
	dbo.wf_api_getWebRequestRightObjectKey(I.id_instance) AS ID_CODEC,
	J.id_job,
	A.id_actionclass, 
	substring(AC.ucode, 17, 1) RIGHTTYPE, 
	I.id_instanceclass
	from wf_instance I with (nolock)
	    join wf_foreignobject FO with (nolock) on FO.id_foreignobject = I.id_foreignobject and FO.ucode='a'
	    join wf_foreignobject FO2 with (nolock) on FO2.id_foreignobject = I.id_foreignobject2 and FO2.ucode='f'
	    join wf_job J with (nolock) on J.id_instance = I.id_instance
	    join wf_action A with (nolock) on J.id_action = A.id_action
	    join wf_actionclass AC with (nolock) on AC.id_actionclass = A.id_actionclass and (AC.ucode like 'af.wiz.3.wbrqst._.act')

===== VIEW dbo.wf_assetWorksheets =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[wf_assetWorksheets]
as
	select 
	I.id_instance,
	I.foreign_key AS ID_FILMATI,
	IC.id_instanceclass,
	IC.friendly_name as INSTANCECLASS_NAME,
	J.id_job,
	J.worker_info,
	J.worker_loginname,
	J.worker_cod_user,
	A.id_action,
	AC.id_actionclass,
	AC.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME,
	AC.data_int as ToAssign,
	AA.Id_anagraf,
	AA.Id_Group,
	AC.id_virtualdocument
	from wf_instance I with (nolock)
	    join wf_foreignobject FO with (nolock) on FO.id_foreignobject = I.id_foreignobject and FO.ucode='f'
	    join wf_job J with (nolock) on J.id_instance = I.id_instance
	    join wf_action A with (nolock) on J.id_action = A.id_action
	    join wf_actionclass AC with (nolock) on AC.id_actionclass = A.id_actionclass and (AC.ucode = 'af.1.qltchk.act' or AC.ucode like 'wks%')
	    join wf_instanceclass IC with (nolock) on IC.id_instanceclass = I.id_instanceclass 
	    left join wf_assignAction AA with (nolock) on AA.id_instance = I.id_instance and AA.id_action = A.id_action and isnull(AA.jobProgress,0)<100

===== VIEW dbo.wf_attachedInstance =====
CREATE   view wf_attachedInstance
as
        select 
            rv.id_foreignobject ID_FOREIGNOBJECT, 
            rv.foreign_key FOREIGN_KEY, 
            rv.id_instanceclass ID_INSTANCECLASS, 
            wi.id_instance ID_INSTANCE, 
            wi.activity_state ACTIVITY_STATE
        from wf_rule4attach rv with (nolock)
            join wf_foreignobject wf with (nolock) on wf.id_foreignobject = rv.id_foreignobject
            left join wf_instance wi with (nolock) on (wi.id_foreignobject = wf.id_foreignobject) and 
                                                      (wi.foreign_key = rv.foreign_key) and 
                                                      (rv.id_instanceclass = wi.id_instanceclass)
        where (wi.id_instance is not null)

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.wf_instance_d_remove_locks =====
CREATE   trigger wf_instance_d_remove_locks
on wf_instance
for delete
--not for replication
as
        declare cr_locks cursor
        read_only
        for select l.[object_name], l.[object_id], l.[object_key], 
                   o.owner_name, o.owner_id, o.owner_key
               from [dbo].[lock_object] l with (nolock)
                   join [dbo].[lock_owner] o with (nolock) on o.id_object = l.id_object
                   join deleted d with (nolock) on d.id_instance = o.[owner_id]
               where  (o.[owner_name] = 'wf_instance')
        declare 
            @lname nvarchar(50), 
            @lid int, 
            @lkey int,
            @oname nvarchar(50), 
            @oid int, 
            @okey int
        open cr_locks
        fetch next from cr_locks into @lname, @lid, @lkey, @oname, @oid, @okey
        while (@@fetch_status = 0)
        begin
          exec [dbo].[lock_release] @lname, @lid, @lkey, @oname, @oid, @okey
          fetch next from cr_locks into @lname, @lid, @lkey, @oname, @oid, @okey
        end
        close cr_locks
        deallocate cr_locks

===== SQL_TRIGGER dbo.wf_instance_u_lastupdate_time =====
CREATE   trigger wf_instance_u_lastupdate_time
on wf_instance
for update
--not for replication
as
  set nocount on
  if (not update(lastupdate_time)) and
     (not update(run_wdog_cnt)) and 
     (not update(tot_update_cnt)) and 
     (not update(start_cnt)) and 
     (not update(deadline)) and 
     (not update(priority)) and 
     (@@nestlevel <= 8) begin
    update wi
    set 
        wi.lastupdate_time = getdate(),
        wi.run_wdog_cnt = inserted.run_wdog_cnt - 1,
        wi.tot_update_cnt = inserted.tot_update_cnt + 1
    from wf_instance wi 
      join inserted on inserted.id_instance = wi.id_instance
  end

===== VIEW dbo.wf_InstanceFO =====
CREATE   view dbo.wf_InstanceFO
as
	select wfi.id_instance, wfw.id_instanceclass, wfw.friendly_name, foreign_object=wfo.ucode, wfi.foreign_key
	, f__cod_progra=f.cod_progra
	, t__cod_progra=t.cod_progra, t__cod_user=t.cod_user, t__data=t.data, t__ora=t.ora, t__livello=t.livello
	, i__id_filmati=i.id_filmati, i__version=i.version, i__markin=i.markin, i__markout=i.markout
	, a__cod_conto=a.cod_conto
	from wf_instanceclass wfw with(nolock)
	join wf_instance wfi with(nolock) on wfi.id_instanceclass=wfw.id_instanceclass
	join wf_foreignobject wfo with(nolock) on wfo.id_foreignobject=wfi.id_foreignobject
	left join filmati f with(nolock) on f.id_filmati=wfi.foreign_key and wfo.ucode='f'
	left join tpalinse t with(nolock) on t.id_tpalinse=wfi.foreign_key and wfo.ucode='t'
	left join finterruzioni i with(nolock) on i.id_interruzioni=wfi.foreign_key and wfo.ucode='i'
	left join anagraf a with(nolock) on a.id_anagraf=wfi.foreign_key and wfo.ucode='a'

===== VIEW dbo.wf_jobqueue =====
CREATE   VIEW wf_jobqueue
as
    select 
        wi.id_instance as ID_INSTANCE,
        wic.id_instanceclass as ID_INSTANCECLASS,
        wic.friendly_name as INSTANCECLASS_NAME,
        wj.id_job as ID_JOB,
        wj.worker_info as JOB_ASSIGNEE,
        wa.id_action as ID_ACTION,
        wac.id_actionclass as ID_ACTIONCLASS,
        wac.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME,
        wac.category1 as ACTIONCLASS_CATEGORY,
        wfo.ucode as FOREIGN_OBJECT_CODE,
        wi.foreign_key AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_KEY
        from wf_instance wi with (nolock)
            join wf_foreignobject wfo with (nolock) on wfo.id_foreignobject = wi.id_foreignobject
            join wf_job wj with (nolock) on wj.id_instance = wi.id_instance
            join wf_action wa with (nolock) on wj.id_action = wa.id_action
            join wf_actionclass wac with (nolock) on wac.id_actionclass = wa.id_actionclass
            join wf_instanceclass wic with (nolock) on wic.id_instanceclass = wi.id_instanceclass

===== VIEW dbo.wf_LogInfo =====
CREATE   view wf_LogInfo
as
    select 
	WI.id_instance as ID_INSTANCE,
	WL.id_log as ID_LOG,
	WA.id_action as ID_ACTION,
	WAC.id_actionclass as ID_ACTIONCLASS,
	WAC.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME,
	WAC.category1 as ACTIONCLASS_CATEGORY,
	WI.foreign_key AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_KEY,
	WL.worker_loginname AS WORKER_LOGINNAME, 
	WS.friendly_name as StateName,
	WL.id_state,
	WL.timestamp,
	WL.result,
	WL.[message],
	WL.os_login,
	WL.hostname,
	WL.program_name,
	WL.hostprocess,
	WL.worker_cod_user,
	WI.id_instanceclass as ID_INSTANCECLASS,
	WFO.Ucode AS FOREIGN_OBJECT_CODE
	from wf_instance	WI with (nolock)
	join wf_log		WL with (nolock) on WL.id_instance = WI.id_instance
	join wf_action	WA with (nolock) on WL.id_action = WA.id_action
	join wf_actionclass 	WAC with (nolock) on WAC.id_actionclass = WA.id_actionclass
	join wf_state		WS with (nolock) on WL.id_state = WS.id_state 
	join wf_foreignobject WFO with (nolock) on WI.id_foreignobject = WFO.id_foreignobject

===== VIEW dbo.wf_objectsSubSet =====
CREATE   view [dbo].[wf_objectsSubSet]
as
	/*
		Fields: 
			objectReference	= field name (e.g. id_filmati)
			objectType		= field type (values list: 'string', 'int', 'datetime', 'bit', 'real')
			objectSubset 		= subset code 
			selectionQuery 	= the query to list all subset items
		
	*/
	select	objectReference = 'id_filmati', 
		objectType = 'int',
		objectSubset = 'system asset', 
		selectionQuery = 'select Id_Filmati objRef, saCode Code, saDescription [Description] from FSystemAssets with (nolock) where Id_Filmati is not null  order by id_filmati, saCode' 
	union
	select	objectReference = 'id_filmati',  
		objectType = 'int',
		objectSubset = 'asset',
		selectionQuery = 'select Id_Filmati objRef, cod_progra Code, descrizio [Description] from filmati with (nolock) where hidden=0 order by cod_progra ' 
	union
	select	objectReference = 'id_codec',  
		objectType = 'int',
		objectSubset = 'codec',
		selectionQuery = 'select Id_codec objRef, [type] Code, descr [Description] from codecs c with (nolock) where isnull(active,0)=1 order by [type]' 
	union
	select	objectReference = 'id_metadevice',  
		objectType = 'int',
		objectSubset = 'device',
		selectionQuery = 'select Id_metadevice objRef, NULL Code, [Description] from fs_metadevice with (nolock) order by isnull(vieworder,1000),[Description]'

===== VIEW dbo.wf_operationsSettings =====
CREATE   view dbo.wf_operationsSettings
as
	/*
		Parameters: 
			Operation			= operation description 
			ToTranslate         = 1: operation contains etereln source value
			KeyName				= inifiles obj_name value
			AllUsers			= 1 all users 0 single user
			ActUcodeConstraint	= workflow selection contraint
								  any workflow that contains an action with ucode LIKE this
								  NULL no constraint
			ActUcodeNegConstraint= workflow selection negative contraint
								  any workflow that contains NO action with ucode LIKE this
								  NULL no negative constraint
								  
		Add a configuration:
			union
			select	Operation = 'Quality check', 
					KeyName = 'global.ini/settings/WF/asset/qualityCheck', 
					AllUsers = '1',
					ActUcodeConstraint = 'af.1.qltchk%', 
					ActUcodeNegConstraint = NULL
											  
	*/
	select	Operation = 'After asset videofile import', ToTranslate=1,
		KeyName = 'global.ini/settings/WF/asset/videofileImport', 
		AllUsers = '1',
		ActUcodeConstraint = NULL, 
		ActUcodeNegConstraint = NULL 
	union
	select	Operation = 'Workflow da lanciare al termine delle registrazioni', ToTranslate=1,
		KeyName = 'Param.ini/ETERE RECORDING/RC_WORKFLOW', 
		AllUsers = '0',
		ActUcodeConstraint = NULL, 
		ActUcodeNegConstraint = NULL
	union

===== VIEW dbo.wf_WorksheetsList =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[wf_WorksheetsList]
as
	select 
		AC.id_actionclass,
		AC.friendly_name as ACTIONCLASS_NAME,
		AC.data_int as ToAssign,
		AC.ucode as ACTIONUCODE,
		A.id_action,
		IC.id_instanceclass,
		IC.friendly_name as INSTANCECLASS_NAME,
		I.id_instance,
		I.foreign_key AS ID_FILMATI,
		S.ucode,
		S.friendly_name as STATE_NAME,
		J.id_job,
		J.worker_info,
		J.worker_loginname,
		J.worker_cod_user,
		AA.id_anagraf,
		AA.datestart,
		AA.dateend,
		AA.note,
		AA.id_assignAction,
		AA.Id_Group,
		AA.Outlook_int_type,
		AA.priorityLevel
	from wf_actionclass AC with (nolock)
	join wf_action A with (nolock) on AC.id_actionclass = A.id_actionclass and AC.ucode like 'wksh.%'
	join wf_instanceclass IC with (nolock) on A.id_instanceclass = IC.id_instanceclass
	join wf_instance I with (nolock) on IC.id_instanceclass = I.id_instanceclass 
	join wf_foreignobject FO with (nolock) on FO.id_foreignobject = I.id_foreignobject and FO.ucode='f'
	left join wf_state S with (nolock) on S.id_state = I.activity_state
	left join wf_job J with (nolock) on J.id_instance = I.id_instance and J.id_action = A.id_action
	left join wf_assignAction AA with (nolock) on AA.id_instance = I.id_instance and AA.id_action = A.id_action
	where isnull(S.ucode,'') <> 'i.term' and isnull(AA.jobProgress,0)<100

===== VIEW dbo.Who_Locks =====
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[Who_Locks] as
	Select P.NT_UserName UserName, P.Program_Name Program, SO.Name TableName, L.Mode, P.Loginame, P.CMD, L.Type
	from master.dbo.sysprocesses P
	join
	(select convert (smallint, req_spid) As spid,
		rsc_dbid As dbid,
		rsc_objid As ObjId,
		rsc_indid As IndId,
		substring (v.name, 1, 4) As Type,
		substring (rsc_text, 1, 16) as Resource,
		substring (u.name, 1, 8) As Mode,
		substring (x.name, 1, 5) As Status
	from 	master.dbo.syslockinfo,
		master.dbo.spt_values v,
		master.dbo.spt_values x,
		master.dbo.spt_values u
	where   master.dbo.syslockinfo.rsc_type = v.number
		and v.type = 'LR'
		and master.dbo.syslockinfo.req_status = x.number
		and x.type = 'LS'
		and master.dbo.syslockinfo.req_mode + 1 = u.number
		and u.type = 'L') L on L.Spid = P.Spid
	join SysObjects SO on SO.Id = L.ObjID
	group by P.NT_UserName, P.Program_Name, SO.Name, L.Mode, P.Loginame, P.Cmd, L.Type

===== VIEW mm.dm_config =====
CREATE   view mm.dm_config
as
        select 
            PROCESSOR_NAME, 
            x.SOURCE_NAME,
            x.DEST_NAME,
            X.CLASS_NAME,
            PROCESSOR_CFG,
            PROCESSOR_USED
        from (
            select
                cast(PROCESSOR_NAME as sysname) as PROCESSOR_NAME,
                cast('<dmProcessor> <param name="Name" value="' + processor_name + '" />' + o.list + '</dmProcessor>' as XML) as PROCESSOR_CFG,
                isnull(p.active, 0) as PROCESSOR_USED
                from ( 
                    select distinct
                    dbo.split(dbo.split(OBJ_NAME, '[', 1), ']', 0) as processor_name
                    from inifiles with (nolock)
                    where OBJ_NAME like 'eteremm2dm.exe.%'
                      and (dbo.split(dbo.split(OBJ_NAME, '[', 1), ']', 0) not in ('ProcessorList', 'Scheduling'))
                ) procs
                cross apply (
                    select
                    substring(dbo.split(param.OBJ_NAME, ']', 1), 2, 4000) as [name],
                    cast(param.OBJ_VALUE as nvarchar(1000)) AS [value]
                    from inifiles param with (nolock) 
                    where param.OBJ_NAME like 'eteremm2dm.exe%'
                      and dbo.split(dbo.split(param.OBJ_NAME, '[', 1), ']', 0) = processor_name
                    FOR XML AUTO
                ) o(list)
                outer apply (
                    select
                      top(1) 1
                      from inifiles with (nolock)
                      where OBJ_NAME like 'EtereMM2dm.exe._ProcessorList_.Processor%' 
                        and cast(OBJ_VALUE as nvarchar(1000)) = PROCESSOR_NAME
                ) p(active)
              ) rawcfg        
          cross apply (
            select 
                n.c.value('./param[@name="Source"][1]/@value', 'nvarchar(max)') as SOURCE_NAME,
                n.c.value('./param[@name="Destination"][1]/@value', 'nvarchar(max)') as DEST_NAME,
                n.c.value('./param[@name="Class"][1]/@value', 'nvarchar(max)') as CLASS_NAME
            from rawcfg.PROCESSOR_CFG.nodes('dmProcessor') n(c)  
            ) x
